+---
+alwaysApply: true
+description: Enforce English-only comments and code
+---
+
+# No Chinese Characters in Code
+
+**All code comments, variable names, function names must be in English.**
+
+- ✅ Allowed: English comments, `.md` files can contain Chinese
+- ❌ Forbidden: Chinese in code comments, docstrings, identifiers
+
+CI check: [check_chinese_comments.sh](mdc:scripts/check_chinese_comments.sh) enforces this rule.
+
+**Important**: Even if user asks in Chinese, generate code with English comments only.

  their  100755 33a9ab836367177edb658961aebdc89bc02f5335 ci/check_chinese_comments.sh
@@ -0,0 +1,18 @@
+#!/bin/bash
+
+echo "Checking for Chinese characters (excluding .md files)..."
+
+export LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
+
+# Use grep with PCRE to detect Chinese characters
+# -I: skip binary files automatically
+# -n: show line numbers
+# -P: use Perl-compatible regex with Unicode support
+if git ls-files | grep -v '\.md$' | xargs -r grep -n -I -P '[\p{Han}]' 2>/dev/null; then
+    echo ""
+    echo "Error: Chinese characters found in code files. Please use English only (Chinese is allowed only in .md files)."
+    exit 1
+fi
+
+echo "Check passed: No Chinese characters found in code files."
+exit 0

+    exit 1
+fi
+
+echo "Check passed: Python format is correct."
+exit 0

+# Purpose of MirrorDataRule:
+# Defines all operations for generating mirrored data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate mirrored files.
+# Format requirements for MirrorDataRule:
+# 1. There are three types of operations for generating mirrored data: scale, resort, swap.
+# 2. scale operation: Multiplies each dimension of the target data by the corresponding scale factor. It has two parameters: the target data name and the scale factor. The scale factor's dimension must match the target data.
+# 3. resort operation: Rearranges the target data according to the given order. It has two parameters: the target data name and the new order. The order's dimension must match the target data.
+# 4. swap operation: Swaps two data items. It has two parameters, and the dimensions of both data items must match.
+MirrorDataRule:
+  - scale: ["root_linear_velocity_in_body", [1, -1, 1]]
+  - scale: ["root_angular_velocity_in_body", [-1, 1, -1]]
+  - resort: ["ankle_pos", [3, 4, 5, 0, 1, 2]]
+  - scale: ["ankle_pos", [1, -1, 1, 1, -1, 1]]
+  - resort: ["ankle_vel", [3, 4, 5, 0, 1, 2]]
+  - scale: ["ankle_vel", [1, -1, 1, 1, -1, 1]]

+# Purpose of SmoothDataRule:
+# Defines all operations for generating smoothed data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate smoothed data.
+# Format requirements for SmoothDataRule:
+# 1. There are five smoothing operations: naive_smooth, quat_smooth, body_vel_diff, body_angvel_diff, naive_diff.
+# 2. naive_smooth: Applies mean filtering to the target data with the given window size. Two parameters: target data name and window size.
+# 3. quat_smooth: Special quaternion mean filtering.
+# 4. body_vel_diff: Special velocity difference calculation.
+# 5. body_angvel_diff: Special angular velocity difference calculation, computes angular velocity from quaternion differences.
+# 6. naive_diff: Computes the first derivative by differencing adjacent data according to the second parameter. Two parameters: result save location and original data before differencing.
+SmoothDataRule:
+  - naive_smooth: ["root_position", 11]
+  - quat_smooth: ["root_quat", 11]
+  - body_vel_diff: ["root_linear_velocity_in_body", "root_position", "root_quat"]
+  - body_angvel_diff: ["root_angular_velocity_in_body", "root_quat"]
+  - naive_smooth: ["ankle_pos", 11]
+  - naive_diff: ["ankle_vel", "ankle_pos"]
+  - naive_smooth: ["leg_L_joint_1_pos", 11]
+  - naive_smooth: ["leg_L_joint_2_pos", 11]

+# Purpose of MirrorDataRule:
+# Defines all operations for generating mirrored data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate mirrored files.
+# Format requirements for MirrorDataRule:
+# 1. There are three types of operations for generating mirrored data: scale, resort, swap.
+# 2. scale operation: Multiplies each dimension of the target data by the corresponding scale factor. It has two parameters: the target data name and the scale factor. The scale factor's dimension must match the target data.
+# 3. resort operation: Rearranges the target data according to the given order. It has two parameters: the target data name and the new order. The order's dimension must match the target data.
+# 4. swap operation: Swaps two data items. It has two parameters, and the dimensions of both data items must match.
+MirrorDataRule:
+  - scale: ["root_linear_velocity_in_body", [1, -1, 1]]
+  - scale: ["root_angular_velocity_in_body", [-1, 1, -1]]
+  - resort: ["ankle_pos", [3, 4, 5, 0, 1, 2]]
+  - scale: ["ankle_pos", [1, -1, 1, 1, -1, 1]]
+  - resort: ["ankle_vel", [3, 4, 5, 0, 1, 2]]

+# Purpose of SmoothDataRule:
+# Defines all operations for generating smoothed data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate smoothed data.
+# Format requirements for SmoothDataRule:
+# 1. There are five smoothing operations: naive_smooth, quat_smooth, body_vel_diff, body_angvel_diff, naive_diff.
+# 2. naive_smooth: Applies mean filtering to the target data with the given window size. Two parameters: target data name and window size.
+# 3. quat_smooth: Special quaternion mean filtering.
+# 4. body_vel_diff: Special velocity difference calculation.
+# 5. body_angvel_diff: Special angular velocity difference calculation, computes angular velocity from quaternion differences.
+# 6. naive_diff: Computes the first derivative by differencing adjacent data according to the second parameter. Two parameters: result save location and original data before differencing.
+SmoothDataRule:
+  - naive_smooth: ["root_position", 11]
+  - quat_smooth: ["root_quat", 11]
+  - body_vel_diff: ["root_linear_velocity_in_body", "root_position", "root_quat"]
+  - body_angvel_diff: ["root_angular_velocity_in_body", "root_quat"]

-# Purpose of MirrorDataRule:
-# Defines all operations for generating mirrored data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate mirrored files.
-# Format requirements for MirrorDataRule:
-# 1. There are three types of operations for generating mirrored data: scale, resort, swap.
-# 2. scale operation: Multiplies each dimension of the target data by the corresponding scale factor. It has two parameters: the target data name and the scale factor. The scale factor's dimension must match the target data.
-# 3. resort operation: Rearranges the target data according to the given order. It has two parameters: the target data name and the new order. The order's dimension must match the target data.
-# 4. swap operation: Swaps two data items. It has two parameters, and the dimensions of both data items must match.
-MirrorDataRule:
-  - scale: ["root_linear_velocity_in_body", [1, -1, 1]]

-# Purpose of SmoothDataRule:
-# Defines all operations for generating smoothed data, so the script can directly read the operation methods and generate smoothed data.
-# Format requirements for SmoothDataRule:
-# 1. There are five smoothing operations: naive_smooth, quat_smooth, body_vel_diff, body_angvel_diff, naive_diff.
-# 2. naive_smooth: Applies mean filtering to the target data with the given window size. Two parameters: target data name and window size.
-# 3. quat_smooth: Special quaternion mean filtering.
-# 4. body_vel_diff: Special velocity difference calculation.
-# 5. body_angvel_diff: Special angular velocity difference calculation, computes angular velocity from quaternion differences.
-# 6. naive_diff: Computes the first derivative by differencing adjacent data according to the second parameter. Two parameters: result save location and original data before differencing.

+    def export_to_onnx(self, obs_input, onnx_path):
+        onnx_net = PolicyNetONNX(self.actor, self.actor_obs_normalizer)
+        # Export the model with a random input
+        input_size = 585  # pt_model.actor[0].in_features
+        if not isinstance(input_size, int):
+            raise ValueError("Only support 1D input")
+        output_size = 10  # pt_model.actor[-1].out_features
+        torch.onnx.export(
+            onnx_net,  # model to be saved
+            obs_input,  # model input (or a tuple for multiple inputs)
+            onnx_path,  # where to save the model
+            input_names=[f"obs_{input_size}"],  # the model's input names
+            output_names=[f"act_{output_size}"],  # the model's output names
+            opset_version=10,
+        )
+
+
+class PolicyNetONNX(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, actor_net, normalizer):
+        super(PolicyNetONNX, self).__init__()
+        self.actor_net = actor_net
+        self.normalizer = normalizer
+        return
+
+    def forward(self, obs):
+        return self.actor_net(self.normalizer(obs))
+
+
+class EmpiricalNormalization(nn.Module):
+    """Normalize mean and variance of values based on empirical values."""
+
+    def __init__(self, shape, eps=1e-2, until=None):
+        """Initialize EmpiricalNormalization module.
+        Args:
+            shape (int or tuple of int): Shape of input values except batch axis.
+            eps (float): Small value for stability.
+            until (int or None): If this arg is specified, the module learns input values until the sum of batch sizes
+            exceeds it.
+
+        Note: The normalization parameters are computed over the whole batch, not for each environment separately.
+        """
+        super().__init__()
+        self.eps = eps
+        self.until = until
+        self.register_buffer('_mean', torch.zeros(shape).unsqueeze(0))
+        self.register_buffer('_var', torch.ones(shape).unsqueeze(0))
+        self.register_buffer('_std', torch.ones(shape).unsqueeze(0))
+        self.register_buffer('count', torch.tensor(0, dtype=torch.long))
+
+    @property
+    def mean(self):
+        return self._mean.squeeze(0).clone()
+
+    @property
+    def std(self):
+        return self._std.squeeze(0).clone()
+
+    def forward(self, x):
+        return (x - self._mean) / (self._std + self.eps)
+
+    @torch.jit.unused
+    def update(self, x):
+        """Learn input values without computing the output values of them"""
+
+        assert self.training, 'Error if call update() during eval()'
+        if self.until is not None and self.count >= self.until:
+            return
+
+        count_x = x.shape[0]
+        self.count += count_x
+        rate = count_x / self.count
+        var_x = torch.var(x, dim=0, unbiased=False, keepdim=True)
+        mean_x = torch.mean(x, dim=0, keepdim=True)
+        delta_mean = mean_x - self._mean
+        self._mean += rate * delta_mean
+        self._var += rate * (var_x - self._var + delta_mean * (mean_x - self._mean))
+        self._std = torch.sqrt(self._var)
+        return

+    def preload_transitions_with_scene_tag(self, num_preload_transitions):
+        """Preload transitions sampled according to scene tag ratios for AMP training"""
+        amp_scene_ratio_info = {}
+        for tag_name, tag_ratio in zip(self.amp_scene_tag_lists, self.amp_scene_tag_ratio):
+            amp_scene_ratio_info[tag_name] = tag_ratio
+        amp_scene_data_time_length = {}
+        for tag_name in self.amp_scene_tag_lists:
+            amp_scene_data_time_length[tag_name] = 0.0
+        for frame_duration, single_traj_tag_info in zip(self.trajectory_frame_durations, self.trajectory_tag_info):
+            for tag_name, tag_info in single_traj_tag_info.items():
+                for start, end in tag_info:
+                    segment_length = frame_duration * (end - start)
+                    amp_scene_data_time_length[tag_name] += segment_length
+        traj_idx_samples = []
+        times_samples = []
+        for idx, frame_duration, single_traj_tag_info in zip(
+            self.trajectory_idxs, self.trajectory_frame_durations, self.trajectory_tag_info
+        ):
+            for tag_name, tag_info in single_traj_tag_info.items():
+                scene_ratio = amp_scene_ratio_info[tag_name]
+                scene_total_time_length = amp_scene_data_time_length[tag_name]
+                for start, end in tag_info:
+                    segment_length = frame_duration * (end - start)
+                    segment_ratio = segment_length / scene_total_time_length
+                    sample_nums = int(num_preload_transitions * scene_ratio * segment_ratio)
+                    if sample_nums == 0:
+                        continue
+                    start_time = start * frame_duration
+                    end_time = (end - 1) * frame_duration
+                    time_length = end_time - start_time
+                    time_choices = time_length * np.random.uniform(size=sample_nums) + start_time
+
+                    traj_idx_samples.extend([idx] * sample_nums)
+                    times_samples.extend(time_choices)
+
+        traj_idxs = np.array(traj_idx_samples)
+        times = np.array(times_samples)
+
+        return traj_idxs, times
+
+    def cleanup_no_scene_tag_transitions(self, traj_idxs, times):
+        """Remove transitions that are not covered by any scene tag"""
+
+        def get_select_item_mask(traj_idxs, times):
+            """Get mask for transitions that fall within scene tag ranges"""
+            p = times / self.trajectory_lens[traj_idxs]
+            n = self.trajectory_num_frames[traj_idxs]
+            idx_low, _ = np.floor(p * n).astype(int), np.ceil(p * n).astype(int)
+            select_item_mask = torch.zeros(len(traj_idxs), dtype=torch.bool)
+            for traj_idx in set(traj_idxs):
+                traj_mask = traj_idxs == traj_idx
+                for _, tag_info in self.trajectory_tag_info[traj_idx].items():
+                    for start, end in tag_info:
+                        select_item_mask = select_item_mask | ((idx_low >= start) & (idx_low < end) & traj_mask)
+            return select_item_mask
+
+        select_item_mask_curr = get_select_item_mask(traj_idxs, times)
+        select_item_mask_next = get_select_item_mask(traj_idxs, times + self.time_between_frames)
+        select_item_mask = select_item_mask_curr & select_item_mask_next
+        indices = torch.nonzero(select_item_mask, as_tuple=False).squeeze(-1)
+        output_traj_idxs = traj_idxs[indices]
+        output_times = times[indices]
+        return output_traj_idxs, output_times
+

+    def filter_dataset_by_redundant_scene_tags(self, all_frame_scene_tags):
+        """Randomly keep only one scene tag per frame when multiple tags exist"""
+        multi_one_mask = (all_frame_scene_tags == 1).sum(dim=1) > 1
+        if multi_one_mask.any():
+            one_indices = torch.where(all_frame_scene_tags[multi_one_mask] == 1)
+            row_groups = torch.unique(one_indices[0], return_counts=True)
+            random_indices = torch.tensor(
+                [torch.randint(0, count, (1,)).item() for count in row_groups[1]], device=self.device
+            )
+            all_frame_scene_tags[multi_one_mask] = 0
+            all_frame_scene_tags[
+                multi_one_mask.nonzero().squeeze(dim=1),
+                one_indices[1][
+                    torch.cumsum(torch.tensor([0] + row_groups[1].tolist()[:-1], device=self.device), 0)
+                    + random_indices
+                ],
+            ] = 1
+
+        if (all_frame_scene_tags.sum(dim=-1) > 1).any():
+            logger.info(f'all_frame_scene_tags: {all_frame_scene_tags}')
+            raise ValueError("all_frame_scene_tags contains rows with more than 1 1")
+
+        if (all_frame_scene_tags.sum(dim=-1) == 0).any():
+            logger.info(f'all_frame_scene_tags: {all_frame_scene_tags}')
+            raise ValueError("all_frame_scene_tags contains error")
+
+        return all_frame_scene_tags

+    def construct_amp_state_base(self):
+        """Construct base AMP state including velocities, joint states, feet states and scene tags"""
+        amp_state = R01AMPStateBase(
+            base_lin_vel=self.base_lin_vel,
+            base_ang_vel=self.base_ang_vel,
+            joint_pos=self.dof_pos,
+            joint_vel=self.dof_vel,
+            feet_pos=self.feet_pos,
+            feet_vel=self.feet_vel,
+            projected_gravity=self.projected_gravity,
+            frame_scene_tags=self.get_walking_amp_scene_tags(),
+        )
+        return amp_state
+
+    def get_walking_amp_scene_tags(self):
+        """Get scene tags for current walking commands (stand, turn, straight, back)"""
+
+        if not (
+            getattr(self.cfg.env, 'amp_add_scene_tags', False) and getattr(self.cfg.env, 'amp_scene_tag_lists', None)
+        ):
+            return None
+
+        amp_tag_dim = len(self.cfg.env.amp_scene_tag_lists) if self.cfg.env.amp_scene_tag_lists is not None else 0
+        frame_scene_tags = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, amp_tag_dim, device=self.device)
+        stand_mask = torch.norm(self.commands[:, :3], dim=1) < 0.1
+        turn_mask = (torch.abs(self.commands[:, 0]) < 0.01) & (torch.abs(self.commands[:, 2]) > 0.01) & (~stand_mask)
+        back_mask = (self.commands[:, 0] <= -0.01) & (~turn_mask) & (~stand_mask)
+        straight_mask = (~stand_mask) & (~turn_mask) & (~back_mask)
+
+        for idx, tag_name in enumerate(self.cfg.env.amp_scene_tag_lists):
+            if tag_name == "stand":
+                frame_scene_tags[stand_mask, idx] = 1
+            elif tag_name == "turn":
+                frame_scene_tags[turn_mask, idx] = 1
+            elif tag_name == "straight":

+    def _resample_commands(self, env_ids):
+        """Resample velocity commands according to scene tag ratios for different motion types"""
+        if not hasattr(self.cfg.env, 'amp_scene_tag_ratio') or not hasattr(
+            self.cfg.commands, 'amp_scene_sample_ranges'
+        ):
+            return super()._resample_commands(env_ids)
+
+        if env_ids.shape[0] == 0:
+            return
+
+        self.commands[env_ids, :] = torch.zeros_like(self.commands[env_ids, :])
+
+        prob_sum = 0.0
+        for tag_name, tag_prob in zip(self.cfg.env.amp_scene_tag_lists, self.cfg.env.amp_scene_tag_ratio):
+            if tag_name == "straight":
+                straight_prob_range = [prob_sum, prob_sum + tag_prob]
+                prob_sum += tag_prob
+            elif tag_name == "back":
+                backward_prob_range = [prob_sum, prob_sum + tag_prob]
+                prob_sum += tag_prob
+            elif tag_name == "stand":
+                stand_prob_range = [prob_sum, prob_sum + tag_prob]
+                prob_sum += tag_prob
+            elif tag_name == "turn":
+                turn_prob_range = [prob_sum, prob_sum + tag_prob]
+                prob_sum += tag_prob
+            else:
+                raise ValueError(f"Invalid tag name: {tag_name}")
+        if not math.isclose(prob_sum, 1.0, rel_tol=1e-9):
+            raise ValueError("The sum of tag_prob values must be 1.0")
+
+        random_prob = torch_rand_float(0.0, 1.0, (len(env_ids), 1), device=self.device)
+        straight_mask = (random_prob >= straight_prob_range[0]) & (random_prob < straight_prob_range[1])
+        if torch.any(straight_mask):
+            straight_env_ids = straight_mask.squeeze(-1).nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()
+            self.commands[env_ids[straight_env_ids], 0] = torch_rand_float(
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.straight_vx_range[0],
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.straight_vx_range[1],
+                (len(straight_env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            ).squeeze(1)
+            randomd_wz = torch_rand_float(
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.straight_wz_range[0],
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.straight_wz_range[1],
+                (len(straight_env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            )
+            randomd_wz = randomd_wz * (
+                torch.abs(randomd_wz) > self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.straight_wz_deadzone
+            ).to(torch.float32)
+            self.commands[env_ids[straight_env_ids], 2] = randomd_wz.squeeze(1)
+
+        backward_mask = (random_prob >= backward_prob_range[0]) & (random_prob < backward_prob_range[1])
+        if torch.any(backward_mask):
+            backward_env_ids = backward_mask.squeeze(-1).nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()
+            self.commands[env_ids[backward_env_ids], 0] = -1.0 * torch_rand_float(
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.backward_vx_range[0],
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.backward_vx_range[1],
+                (len(backward_env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            ).squeeze(1)
+            randomd_wz = torch_rand_float(
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.backward_wz_range[0],
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.backward_wz_range[1],
+                (len(backward_env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            )
+            randomd_wz = randomd_wz * (
+                torch.abs(randomd_wz) > self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.backward_wz_deadzone
+            ).to(torch.float32)
+            self.commands[env_ids[backward_env_ids], 2] = randomd_wz.squeeze(1)
+
+        stand_mask = (random_prob >= stand_prob_range[0]) & (random_prob < stand_prob_range[1])
+        if torch.any(stand_mask):
+            stand_env_ids = stand_mask.squeeze(-1).nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()
+            self.commands[env_ids[stand_env_ids], :] = 0.0
+
+        turn_mask = (random_prob >= turn_prob_range[0]) & (random_prob < turn_prob_range[1])
+        if torch.any(turn_mask):
+            turn_env_ids = turn_mask.squeeze(-1).nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()
+            randomd_wz = torch_rand_float(
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.turn_wz_range[0],
+                self.cfg.commands.amp_scene_sample_ranges.turn_wz_range[1],
+                (len(turn_env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            )
+            signs = torch.randint(0, 2, (len(turn_env_ids), 1), device=self.device) * 2 - 1
+            randomd_wz = randomd_wz * signs
+            self.commands[env_ids[turn_env_ids], 2] = randomd_wz.squeeze(1)
+
+        self.reset_base_vel_history(env_ids)

+    def _reward_tracking_avg_lin_vel(self):
+        """Reward for tracking linear velocity commands using average velocity with adaptive sigma"""
+        lin_vel_error = torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, :2] - self.base_avg_vel[:, :2]), dim=1)
+        stand_mask = torch.norm(self.commands[:, :3], dim=1) < 0.1
+        rotate_in_place_mask = (
+            (torch.abs(self.commands[:, 0]) < 0.01) & (torch.abs(self.commands[:, 2]) > 0.01) & (~stand_mask)
+        )
+        tracking_sigma_tensor = (
+            torch.ones_like(rotate_in_place_mask).to(torch.float32) * self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_lin_vel
+        )
+        tracking_sigma_tensor[rotate_in_place_mask] = self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_lin_vel_for_rotate_in_place
+        return torch.exp(-lin_vel_error / tracking_sigma_tensor)

+def calculate_arm_range_metric(data: RobotInputData) -> Dict[str, float]:
+    """
+    Compute average range of motion for left/right elbow and shoulder pitch angles.
+    Styled after calculate_hip_pitch_vel_metric.
+    """
+
+    def calc_angle_range(angle_data: np.ndarray, start_idx: int, end_idx: int) -> float:
+        # Max minus min within the segment
+        if end_idx <= start_idx:
+            return 0.0
+        segment = angle_data[start_idx:end_idx]
+        if len(segment) == 0:
+            return 0.0
+        return float(np.max(segment) - np.min(segment))
+
+    def calculate_metric(data: RobotInputData, target_command: float) -> Dict:
+        left_elbow_range = 0.0
+        right_elbow_range = 0.0
+        left_shoulder_range = 0.0
+        right_shoulder_range = 0.0
+        count = 0
+
+        for start_idx, end_idx in split_data_by_command(data.command_vx, data.command_dyaw, target_command, 0.0):
+            left_elbow_range += calc_angle_range(data.arm_l_elbow_pitch_angle, start_idx, end_idx)
+            right_elbow_range += calc_angle_range(data.arm_r_elbow_pitch_angle, start_idx, end_idx)
+            left_shoulder_range += calc_angle_range(data.arm_l_shoulder_pitch_angle, start_idx, end_idx)
+            right_shoulder_range += calc_angle_range(data.arm_r_shoulder_pitch_angle, start_idx, end_idx)
+            count += 1
+
+        if count == 0:
+            return {
+                f"arm_elbow_pitch_range_avg{target_command}": 0.0,
+                f"arm_shoulder_pitch_range_avg{target_command}": 0.0,
+            }
+
+        elbow_range_avg = ((left_elbow_range + right_elbow_range) / 2) / 3.141592 * 180 / count
+        shoulder_range_avg = ((left_shoulder_range + right_shoulder_range) / 2) / 3.141592 * 180 / count
+        return {
+            f"arm_elbow_pitch_range_avg{target_command}": elbow_range_avg,
+            f"arm_shoulder_pitch_range_avg{target_command}": shoulder_range_avg,
+        }
+
+    temp_metric_dict = {}
+    temp_metric_dict.update(calculate_metric(data, 0.3))
+    temp_metric_dict.update(calculate_metric(data, 0.4))
+    temp_metric_dict.update(calculate_metric(data, 0.6))
+    temp_metric_dict.update(calculate_metric(data, 0.8))
+
+    return temp_metric_dict
+
+

+# Sim2Real 测试系统使用说明
+
+## 概述
+
+本系统用于生成仿真测试数据，通过运行仿真器（`sim_r01_v12.py`）和控制器（`ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py`）来测试不同PD参数组合下的关节响应。
+
+### 系统架构
+
+```
+sim_r01_v12.py (仿真器)  <--LCM通信-->  ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py (控制器)
+     |                                           |
+     |                                           |
+     └────────── Isaac Gym 物理仿真 ────────────┘
+                              |
+                              └──> 生成CSV数据文件
+```
+
+## 运行流程
+
+### 1. 启动仿真器
+
+首先在一个终端中运行仿真器：
+
+```bash
+cd humanoid-gym/humanoid/test
+python sim_r01_v12.py
+```
+
+仿真器将：
+- 初始化Isaac Gym环境
+- 加载机器人模型
+- 等待控制器连接（通过LCM）
+
+### 2. 启动控制器
+
+在另一个终端中运行控制器：
+
+```bash
+cd humanoid-gym/humanoid/test
+python ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py
+```
+
+控制器将：
+- 通过LCM连接到仿真器
+- 根据配置的PD参数列表自动测试
+- 生成CSV数据文件到 `joint_{index}/` 文件夹
+
+## 配置说明
+
+### 测试部位配置
+
+在 `ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py` 的 `__init__` 方法中配置：
+
+```python
+self.leg_index = 0      # 0=左腿, 1=右腿
+self.arm_index = -1    # 0=左臂, 1=右臂, -1=不测试
+self.waist_index = -1   # 0=腰, -1=不测试
+self.neck_index = -1   # 0=颈, -1=不测试
+self.joint_index = 0   # 当前测试的关节索引（0-5用于腿，0-4用于腰，0-6用于臂）
+```
+
+**注意**：
+- 每次只能测试一个部位（leg/arm/waist/neck）
+- `-1` 表示不测试该部位
+- `joint_index` 表示该部位内起始的关节索引
+
+### PD参数列表配置
+
+在 `ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py` 的 `__init__` 方法中配置：
+
+```python
+# 为每个关节定义kp和kd参数列表
+self.joint_kp_list = [[200], [200], [200], [200], [200], [200], [200]]
+self.joint_kd_list = [[100], [50], [50], [50], [50], [50], [50]]
+```
+
+**说明**：
+- `joint_kp_list[i]` 和 `joint_kd_list[i]` 分别对应 `joint_index=i` 的kp和kd参数列表
+- 系统会自动生成所有kp和kd的组合进行测试
+- 例如：`kp_list=[200, 300]`, `kd_list=[50, 100]` 会生成4种组合：
+  - (kp=200, kd=50)
+  - (kp=200, kd=100)
+  - (kp=300, kd=50)
+  - (kp=300, kd=100)
+
+### 正弦运动参数配置
+
+#### 腿部测试参数
+
+在 `update_controller` 方法中配置：
+
+```python
+# 左腿和右腿各6个关节的默认位置
+leg_pos_default_left = [-0.1, -0.075, -0.1, 0.8, -0.2, 0]
+leg_pos_default_right = [0.1, 0.075, -0.1, 0.8, -0.2, 0]
+
+# 左腿和右腿各6个关节的默认PD参数
+leg_kp_default_left = [100, 100, 100, 100, 100, 100]
+leg_kp_default_right = [100, 100, 100, 100, 100, 100]
+leg_kd_default_left = [100, 100, 100, 50, 20, 20]
+leg_kd_default_right = [100, 100, 100, 50, 20, 20]
+
+# 正弦运动幅值（弧度）
+leg_joint_amplitude = [
+    20 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 0
+    20 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 1
+    25 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 2
+    40 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 3
+    20 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 4
+    20 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 5
+]
+
+# 正弦运动频率
+self.freq = 0.5  # Hz
+```
+
+#### 腰部测试参数
+
+```python
+# 腰部5个关节的默认位置
+waist_pos_default = [0.0, 0.1745, 0.1745, 0.0, 0.0]
+
+# 腰部5个关节的默认PD参数
+waist_kp_default = [2500, 3500, 3500, 3500, 2500]
+waist_kd_default = [50, 100, 50, 50, 50]
+
+# 腰部5个关节的初始偏移和幅值
+waist_joint_offset = [0.0, 0.0698, 0.1745, 0.0, 0.0]
+waist_joint_amplitude = [0.4014, 0.2269, 0.2094, 0.3316, 0.2967]
+```
+
+#### 手臂测试参数
+
+```python
+# 左臂和右臂各7个关节的默认位置
+arm_pos_default_left = [0, 0.5236, 0, -0.5236, 0, 0, 0]
+arm_pos_default_right = [0, -0.5236, 0, -0.5236, 0, 0, 0]
+
+# 左臂和右臂各7个关节的默认PD参数
+arm_kp_default_left = [2000, 1500, 3000, 1500, 2200, 700, 700]
+arm_kp_default_right = [2000, 1500, 3000, 1500, 2200, 700, 700]
+arm_kd_default_left = [30, 30, 50, 20, 30, 10, 10]
+arm_kd_default_right = [30, 30, 50, 20, 30, 10, 10]
+
+# 左臂和右臂各7个关节的初始偏移和幅值
+arm_offset_left = [-0.15, 0.1, -0.05, -0.125, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0]
+arm_offset_right = [-0.15, -0.1, 0.05, -0.125, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0]
+arm_joint_amplitude = [
+    16 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 0
+    7 / 180 * np.pi,   # joint 1
+    30 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 2
+    5 / 180 * np.pi,   # joint 3
+    11 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 4
+    10 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 5
+    10 / 180 * np.pi,  # joint 6
+]
+```
+
+## PD参数测试逻辑
+
+### 测试流程
+
+1. **初始化阶段**：
+   - 根据 `joint_index` 获取对应的 `kp_list` 和 `kd_list`
+   - 生成所有PD参数组合（`control_params_list`）
+   - 计算测试用例总数：`test_case_num = len(kp_list) * len(kd_list)`
+
+2. **测试循环**：
+   - 每10000个仿真步为一个测试周期
+   - 使用 `debug_current_index` 选择当前测试的PD参数组合
+   - 在第9999步时保存数据（保存最近4000个数据点）
+
+3. **数据保存**：
+   - 文件命名格式：`sim_p_{kp}_d_{kd}.csv`
+   - 保存路径：`joint_{joint_index}/sim_p_{kp}_d_{kd}.csv`
+   - 保存的数据包括：
+     - 时间戳 (`ts`)
+     - 关节位置 (`leg_joint_pos_gym_*`)
+     - 关节速度 (`leg_joint_vel_gym_*`)
+     - 目标位置 (`target_leg_joint_pos_gym_*`)
+     - 其他部位的状态（waist, arm, neck）
+
+4. **自动切换**：
+   - 完成所有PD参数组合测试后，自动切换到下一个关节
+   - `joint_index += 1`
+   - 重新初始化PD参数列表
+   - 当 `joint_index == 6` 时（对于腿部），程序自动退出
+
+
+
+## 输出数据格式
+
+### CSV文件结构
+
+每个CSV文件包含以下列：
+
+- `ts`: 仿真时间戳
+- `leg_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `leg_joint_pos_gym_11`: 12个腿部关节位置
+- `leg_joint_vel_gym_0` ~ `leg_joint_vel_gym_11`: 12个腿部关节速度
+- `waist_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `waist_joint_pos_gym_4`: 5个腰部关节位置
+- `waist_joint_vel_gym_0` ~ `waist_joint_vel_gym_4`: 5个腰部关节速度
+- `arm_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `arm_joint_pos_gym_13`: 14个手臂关节位置
+- `arm_joint_vel_gym_0` ~ `arm_joint_vel_gym_13`: 14个手臂关节速度
+- `target_leg_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `target_leg_joint_pos_gym_11`: 12个腿部目标位置
+- `target_waist_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `target_waist_joint_pos_gym_4`: 5个腰部目标位置
+- `target_arm_joint_pos_gym_0` ~ `target_arm_joint_pos_gym_13`: 14个手臂目标位置
+
+### 文件命名规则
+
+- 格式：`sim_p_{kp}_d_{kd}.csv`
+- 示例：`sim_p_200_d_50.csv` 表示 kp=200, kd=50 的测试数据
+
+### 数据保存位置
+
+```
+humanoid-gym/humanoid/test/
+├── joint_0/
+│   ├── sim_p_200_d_50.csv
+│   ├── sim_p_200_d_100.csv
+│   └── ...
+├── joint_1/
+│   ├── sim_p_200_d_50.csv
+│   └── ...
+└── ...
+```
+
+## 配置示例
+
+### 示例1：测试左腿关节0，多个PD参数组合
+
+```python
+self.leg_index = 0
+self.arm_index = -1
+self.waist_index = -1
+self.joint_index = 0
+
+# 测试3个kp值和2个kd值的所有组合（共6种）
+self.joint_kp_list = [[200, 300, 400], [200], [200], [200], [200], [200], [200]]
+self.joint_kd_list = [[50, 100], [50], [50], [50], [50], [50], [50]]
+```
+
+### 示例2：测试腰部关节2
+
+```python
+self.leg_index = -1
+self.arm_index = -1
+self.waist_index = 0
+self.joint_index = 2
+
+# 测试2个kp值和2个kd值的所有组合（共4种）
+self.joint_kp_list = [[200], [200], [3500, 4000], [200], [200], [200], [200]]
+self.joint_kd_list = [[50], [50], [50, 100], [50], [50], [50], [50]]
+```
+
+### 示例3：测试左臂关节3
+
+```python
+self.leg_index = -1
+self.arm_index = 0
+self.waist_index = -1
+self.joint_index = 3
+
+# 测试多个PD参数组合
+self.joint_kp_list = [[200], [200], [200], [1500, 2000, 2500], [200], [200], [200]]
+self.joint_kd_list = [[50], [50], [50], [20, 30, 40], [50], [50], [50]]
+```
+
+## 注意事项
+
+1. **运行顺序**：必须先启动仿真器，再启动控制器
+2. **LCM通信**：确保LCM正常工作，两个程序能够通信
+3. **测试时间**：每个PD参数组合测试10000步（约20秒，假设dt=0.002s）
+4. **数据保存**：只保存每个测试周期的最后4000个数据点
+5. **自动退出**：当测试完所有关节后（`joint_index == 6`），程序会自动退出
+6. **UDP通信**：控制器还会通过UDP（127.0.0.1:9870）发送实时数据，可用于实时监控
+
+## 故障排除
+
+### 问题1：仿真器和控制器无法通信
+
+**解决**：
+- 检查LCM是否正确安装
+- 确保两个程序在同一台机器上运行
+- 检查防火墙设置
+
+### 问题2：数据文件未生成
+
+**解决**：
+- 确保程序运行足够长时间（至少10000步）
+- 检查 `joint_{index}/` 文件夹是否存在写入权限
+- 查看控制台输出，确认测试进度
+
+### 问题3：测试参数未生效
+
+**解决**：
+- 检查 `joint_index` 是否与 `joint_kp_list` 和 `joint_kd_list` 的索引对应
+- 确认 `leg_index`/`arm_index`/`waist_index` 设置正确
+- 查看控制台输出，确认当前使用的PD参数
+
+## 相关文件
+
+- `sim_r01_v12.py`: Isaac Gym仿真器
+- `ctl_r01_v12_sim2real.py`: 控制器和数据记录器
+- `cfg_r01_v12_sim2real.py`: 配置文件
+- `cfg_r01_v12.py`: 仿真器配置文件
added in remote
  their  100644 5fbbcd99b0646f194f087dd55b5ab797e6af0ee3 humanoid-gym/humanoid/test/cfg_r01_v111.py
@@ -0,0 +1,416 @@
+from isaacgym import gymapi, gymutil
+from scipy.spatial.transform import Rotation
+from scipy.linalg import block_diag
+import numpy as np
+
+
+class ConfigModule:
+    def __init__(self):
+        # sim
+        self.physics = gymapi.SIM_PHYSX
+        self.sim_params = gymapi.SimParams()
+        self.sim_params.dt = 1 / 500
+        self.sim_params.substeps = 1
+        self.sim_params.gravity = gymapi.Vec3(0.0, 0.0, -9.81)
+        self.sim_params.physx.num_threads = 1
+        self.sim_params.physx.use_gpu = False
+        self.sim_params.physx.solver_type = 1
+        self.sim_params.physx.contact_offset = 0.01
+        self.sim_params.physx.rest_offset = 0.0
+        self.sim_params.physx.num_position_iterations = 4
+        self.sim_params.physx.num_velocity_iterations = 0
+        self.sim_params.up_axis = gymapi.UP_AXIS_Z
+        self.sim_params.use_gpu_pipeline = False
+
+        # ground
+        self.plane_params = gymapi.PlaneParams()
+        self.plane_params.normal = gymapi.Vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0)
+        self.plane_params.static_friction = 1.0
+        self.plane_params.dynamic_friction = 1.0
+
+        # viewer
+        self.camera_properties = gymapi.CameraProperties()
+        self.camera_properties.width = 1600
+        self.camera_properties.height = 900
+        self.keyboard_event_dict = {
+            gymapi.KEY_A: "RESET_ALL",
+            gymapi.KEY_R: "RESET_ACTOR",
+            gymapi.KEY_Q: "ESCAPE",
+            gymapi.KEY_H: "HOLD",
+            gymapi.KEY_C: "CAMERA",
