+#!/bin/bash
+# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
+#
+# Unified data analysis entry script (Bash version)
+#
+# Features:
+# 1. Environment check and automatic dependency installation
+# 2. Unified body-part selection (only select once)
+# 3. Run compute_torque.py and plot_phase.py sequentially
+#
+# Usage:
+#     bash analyze_data.sh [data_path] [--mode MODE] [--skip-torque] [--skip-plot]
+#
+# Arguments:
+#     data_path: data path (default: ./data)
+#     --mode: plot mode (default: individual)
+#     --skip-torque: skip torque computation
+#     --skip-plot: skip phase plotting
+
+set -e # exit immediately on error
+
+# Color definitions
+RED='\033[0;31m'
+GREEN='\033[0;32m'
+YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
+BLUE='\033[0;34m'
+NC='\033[0m' # No Color
+
+# Get script directory
+SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
+cd "$SCRIPT_DIR"
+
+# Default arguments
+DATA_PATH="./data"
+MODE="individual"
+SKIP_TORQUE=false
+SKIP_PLOT=false
+
+# Parse command line arguments
+while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
+    case $1 in
+    --mode)
+        MODE="$2"
+        shift 2
+        ;;
+    --skip-torque)
+        SKIP_TORQUE=true
+        shift
+        ;;
+    --skip-plot)
+        SKIP_PLOT=true
+        shift
+        ;;
+    --help | -h)
+        echo "Usage: $0 [data_path] [options]"
+        echo ""
+        echo "Arguments:"
+        echo "  data_path              data path (default: ./data)"
+        echo ""
+        echo "Options:"
+        echo "  --mode MODE            plot mode: individual, compare, left_right_compare, target_compare (default: individual)"
+        echo "  --skip-torque          skip torque computation"
+        echo "  --skip-plot            skip phase plotting"
+        echo "  --help, -h             show this help message"
+        echo ""
+        echo "Examples:"
+        echo "  $0 ./data"
+        echo "  $0 ./data --mode compare"
+        echo "  $0 ./data --skip-plot"
+        exit 0
+        ;;
+    -*)
+        echo -e "${RED}Error: unknown option $1${NC}"
+        exit 1
+        ;;
+    *)
+        DATA_PATH="$1"
+        shift
+        ;;
+    esac
+done
+
+# Print welcome message
+echo "================================================================================"
+echo "Unified data analysis entry script (Bash version)"
+echo "================================================================================"
+echo "OS:        $(uname -s) $(uname -r)"
+echo "Data path: $(realpath "$DATA_PATH" 2>/dev/null || echo "$DATA_PATH")"
+echo "Plot mode: $MODE"
+echo "================================================================================"
+
+# Check data path
+if [ ! -d "$DATA_PATH" ]; then
+    echo -e "${RED}Error: data path does not exist: $DATA_PATH${NC}"
+    exit 1
+fi
+
+# Check Python environment
+echo ""
+echo "[1/4] Checking environment..."
+
+# Detect Python command
+if command -v python3 &>/dev/null; then
+    PYTHON_CMD="python3"
+elif command -v python &>/dev/null; then
+    PYTHON_CMD="python"
+else
+    echo -e "${RED}Error: Python interpreter not found${NC}"
+    echo "Please install Python 3.6 or newer"
+    exit 1
+fi
+
+# Check Python version
+PYTHON_VERSION=$($PYTHON_CMD --version 2>&1 | awk '{print $2}')
+echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Python version: $PYTHON_VERSION"
+
+# Check pip
+if command -v pip3 &>/dev/null; then
+    PIP_CMD="pip3"
+elif command -v pip &>/dev/null; then
+    PIP_CMD="pip"
+else
+    echo -e "${YELLOW}Warning: pip not found, trying to install...${NC}"
+    if [ "$PYTHON_CMD" = "python3" ]; then
+        sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install -y python3-pip 2>/dev/null ||
+            sudo yum install -y python3-pip 2>/dev/null ||
+            echo -e "${RED}Error: failed to install pip automatically, please install it manually${NC}" && exit 1
+        PIP_CMD="pip3"
+    else
+        echo -e "${RED}Error: please install pip manually${NC}"
+        exit 1
+    fi
+fi
+
+echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} pip found"
+
+# Check and install dependencies
+REQUIRED_PACKAGES=("pandas" "numpy" "matplotlib" "scipy")
+MISSING_PACKAGES=()
+
+echo "Checking required Python packages..."
+for package in "${REQUIRED_PACKAGES[@]}"; do
+    if $PYTHON_CMD -c "import $package" 2>/dev/null; then
+        echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} $package is already installed"
+    else
+        echo -e "${YELLOW}✗${NC} $package is not installed"
+        MISSING_PACKAGES+=("$package")
+    fi
+done
+
+# Install missing packages
+if [ ${#MISSING_PACKAGES[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
+    echo ""
+    echo -e "${YELLOW}Missing dependencies detected, installing...${NC}"
+    echo "Missing packages: ${MISSING_PACKAGES[*]}"
+
+    # Try user-level installation first (no sudo)
+    if $PIP_CMD install --user "${MISSING_PACKAGES[@]}" 2>/dev/null; then
+        echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Dependencies installed successfully (user mode)"
+    # If user install fails, try system-wide install (requires sudo)
+    elif sudo $PIP_CMD install "${MISSING_PACKAGES[@]}" 2>/dev/null; then
+        echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Dependencies installed successfully (system mode)"
+    else
+        echo -e "${RED}Error: failed to install dependencies${NC}"
+        echo "Please run manually: $PIP_CMD install ${MISSING_PACKAGES[*]}"
+        exit 1
+    fi
+
+    # Verify installation
+    echo "Verifying installation..."
+    for package in "${MISSING_PACKAGES[@]}"; do
+        if $PYTHON_CMD -c "import $package" 2>/dev/null; then
+            echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} $package installed successfully"
+        else
+            echo -e "${RED}✗${NC} $package installation failed"
+            exit 1
+        fi
+    done
+fi
+
+echo ""
+echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Environment check passed"
+
+# Interactive body-part selection
+echo ""
+echo "[2/4] Select body part..."
+echo "============================================================"
+echo "Please select the body part corresponding to the data:"
+echo "============================================================"
+echo "1. Left leg  (left_leg)"
+echo "2. Right leg (right_leg)"
+echo "3. Left arm  (left_arm)"
+echo "4. Right arm (right_arm)"
+echo "5. Waist     (waist)"
+echo "============================================================"
+
+while true; do
+    read -p "Please enter your choice (1-5): " choice
+    case $choice in
+    1)
+        BODY_PART="left_leg"
+        break
+        ;;
+    2)
+        BODY_PART="right_leg"
+        break
+        ;;
+    3)
+        BODY_PART="left_arm"
+        break
+        ;;
+    4)
+        BODY_PART="right_arm"
+        break
+        ;;
+    5)
+        BODY_PART="waist"
+        break
+        ;;
+    *)
+        echo -e "${YELLOW}Invalid option, please enter a number between 1 and 5${NC}"
+        ;;
+    esac
+done
+
+echo ""
+echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Selected body part: $BODY_PART"
+
+# Run torque computation
+SUCCESS_COUNT=0
+TOTAL_TASKS=0
+
+if [ "$SKIP_TORQUE" = false ]; then
+    TOTAL_TASKS=$((TOTAL_TASKS + 1))
+    echo ""
+    echo "[3/4] Running torque computation..."
+    echo "================================================================================"
+    echo "Command: $PYTHON_CMD compute_torque.py \"$DATA_PATH\" --body-part $BODY_PART"
+    echo "================================================================================"
+    echo ""
+
+    if $PYTHON_CMD compute_torque.py "$DATA_PATH" --body-part "$BODY_PART"; then
+        SUCCESS_COUNT=$((SUCCESS_COUNT + 1))
+        echo ""
+        echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Torque computation finished"
+    else
+        echo ""
+        echo -e "${RED}✗${NC} Torque computation failed"
+    fi
+else
+    echo ""
+    echo "[3/4] Skipping torque computation"
+fi
+
+# Run phase plotting
+if [ "$SKIP_PLOT" = false ]; then
+    TOTAL_TASKS=$((TOTAL_TASKS + 1))
+    echo ""
+    echo "[4/4] Running phase plotting..."
+    echo "================================================================================"
+    echo "Command: $PYTHON_CMD plot_phase.py \"$DATA_PATH\" --mode $MODE --body-part $BODY_PART"
+    echo "================================================================================"
+    echo ""
+
+    if $PYTHON_CMD plot_phase.py "$DATA_PATH" --mode "$MODE" --body-part "$BODY_PART"; then
+        SUCCESS_COUNT=$((SUCCESS_COUNT + 1))
+        echo ""
+        echo -e "${GREEN}✓${NC} Phase plotting finished"
+    else
+        echo ""
+        echo -e "${RED}✗${NC} Phase plotting failed"
+    fi
+else
+    echo ""
+    echo "[4/4] Skipping phase plotting"
+fi
+
+# Summary
+echo ""
+echo "================================================================================"
+echo "All tasks finished"
+echo "================================================================================"
+echo "Succeeded:  $SUCCESS_COUNT/$TOTAL_TASKS tasks"
+echo "Body part:  $BODY_PART"
+echo "Data path:  $(realpath "$DATA_PATH" 2>/dev/null || echo "$DATA_PATH")"
+echo "================================================================================"
+
+# Exit code based on results
+if [ $TOTAL_TASKS -gt 0 ] && [ $SUCCESS_COUNT -lt $TOTAL_TASKS ]; then
+    exit 1
+elif [ $TOTAL_TASKS -eq 0 ]; then
+    echo ""
+    echo -e "${YELLOW}Warning: all tasks were skipped${NC}"
+    exit 1
+fi
+
+exit 0

+import pandas as pd
+import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
+import sys
+import argparse
+import os
+import re
+import numpy as np
+from scipy.signal import find_peaks
+from matplotlib.backends.backend_pdf import PdfPages
+
+
+def find_complete_period(target_data):
+    """
+    Find one complete period in the position (target) data.
+    Return the start and end indices of the period.
+    """
+    # Find all peak indices in target data
+    peaks, _ = find_peaks(target_data, distance=50)  # distance parameter can be tuned for different data
+
+    if len(peaks) < 2:
+        # If not enough peaks are found, try valleys
+        peaks, _ = find_peaks(-target_data, distance=50)
+        if len(peaks) < 2:
+            raise ValueError("Cannot find a complete period in the data")
+
+    # Return the start and end indices of the first complete period
+    return peaks[0], peaks[2]
+
+
+def extract_joint_number(folder_name):
+    """
+    Extract the joint index from a folder name.
+
+    Args:
+        folder_name: folder name in the format 'joint_{number}'.
+
+    Returns:
+        int: joint index or None if the format does not match.
+    """
+    pattern = r'joint_(\d+)'
+    match = re.match(pattern, folder_name)
+
+    if match:
+        return int(match.group(1))
+    else:
+        return None
+
+
+def extract_parameters_from_filename(filename):
+    """
+    Extract parameter information and tag from a file name.
+
+    Args:
+        filename: file name, format '{sim/real}_p_{kp}_d_{kd}...' (extra suffix is allowed).
+
+    Returns:
+        tuple: (data_type, kp, kd, tag) or None if the format does not match.
+    """
+    pattern = r'^(sim|real)_p_(\d+)_d_(\d+)(.*)'
+    match = re.match(pattern, filename)
+
+    if match:
+        data_type = match.group(1)  # 'sim' or 'real'
+        kp = int(match.group(2))
+        kd = int(match.group(3))
+        tag = match.group(4).strip()  # extract tag (remove leading/trailing spaces)
+        return data_type, kp, kd, tag
+    else:
+        return None
+
+
+def select_body_part():
+    """
+    Interactively select a body part.
+
+    Returns:
+        str: selected body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
+    print("Please select the body part corresponding to the data:")
+    print("=" * 60)
+    print("1. Left leg  (left_leg)")
+    print("2. Right leg (right_leg)")
+    print("3. Left arm  (left_arm)")
+    print("4. Right arm (right_arm)")
+    print("5. Waist     (waist)")
+    print("=" * 60)
+
+    while True:
+        try:
+            choice = input("Please enter your choice (1-5): ").strip()
+            if choice == '1':
+                return 'left_leg'
+            elif choice == '2':
+                return 'right_leg'
+            elif choice == '3':
+                return 'left_arm'
+            elif choice == '4':
+                return 'right_arm'
+            elif choice == '5':
+                return 'waist'
+            else:
+                print("Invalid option, please enter a number between 1 and 5.")
+        except (EOFError, KeyboardInterrupt):
+            print("\n\nOperation cancelled.")
+            sys.exit(0)
+
+
+def get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, body_part):
+    """
+    Get torque and target column names for a given joint index and body part.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+
+    Returns:
+        tuple: (torque_column_name, target_column_name).
+    """
+    if body_part == 'left_leg':
+        torque_col = f'/joint_state/leg_l_joint_state_open_chain/torque[{joint_index}]'
+        target_col = f'/leg_joint_control_test/leg_l_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+    elif body_part == 'right_leg':
+        torque_col = f'/joint_state/leg_r_joint_state_open_chain/torque[{joint_index}]'
+        target_col = f'/leg_joint_control_test/leg_r_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+    elif body_part == 'left_arm':
+        torque_col = f'/joint_state/arm_l_joint_state_open_chain/torque[{joint_index}]'
+        target_col = f'/arm_test/arm_l_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+    elif body_part == 'right_arm':
+        torque_col = f'/joint_state/arm_r_joint_state_open_chain/torque[{joint_index}]'
+        target_col = f'/arm_test/arm_r_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+    elif body_part == 'waist':
+        torque_col = f'/joint_state/waist_joint_state_open_chain/torque[{joint_index}]'
+        target_col = f'/waist_test/waist_joint_target_.position[{joint_index}]'
+    else:
+        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported body part: {body_part}")
+
+    return torque_col, target_col
+
+
+def parse_data_path(arg):
+    """Parse and validate the data path argument."""
+    if not os.path.isdir(arg):
+        raise argparse.ArgumentTypeError(f"Path does not exist: '{arg}'")
+    return arg
+
+
+def find_joint_folders(data_path):
+    """
+    Find all folders in the given path that match the pattern 'joint_{number}'.
+
+    Args:
+        data_path: root data path.
+
+    Returns:
+        list: list of tuples (joint_folder_path, joint_index).
+    """
+    joint_folders = []
+    for item in os.listdir(data_path):
+        item_path = os.path.join(data_path, item)
+        if os.path.isdir(item_path) and item.startswith('joint_'):
+            joint_index = extract_joint_number(item)
+            if joint_index is not None:
+                joint_folders.append((item_path, joint_index))
+
+    return sorted(joint_folders, key=lambda x: x[1])  # sort by joint index
+
+
+def compute_torque_rms_for_files(joint_folder_path, joint_index, body_part, output_to_file=True):
+    """
+    Compute RMS, max, min torque over one complete period for all files in the joint folder.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+        output_to_file: whether to write results to a text file.
+
+    Returns:
+        bool: True if at least one file is processed successfully.
+    """
+    # Get all CSV files
+    csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(joint_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not csv_files:
+        print(f"Warning: no CSV files found in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Prepare output content
+    output_lines = []
+    output_lines.append(f"{'='*80}")
+    output_lines.append(f"Joint {joint_index} - Torque Statistics for Complete Period")
+    output_lines.append(f"Body Part: {body_part}")
+    output_lines.append(f"{'='*80}")
+    output_lines.append(f"{'File':<45} {'kp':<6} {'kd':<6} {'RMS':<12} {'Max':<12} {'Min':<12} {'Period':<10}")
+    output_lines.append(f"{'-'*80}")
+
+    # Also print to console
+    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+    print(f"Joint {joint_index} - Torque Statistics for Complete Period")
+    print(f"Body Part: {body_part}")
+    print(f"{'='*80}")
+    print(f"{'File':<45} {'kp':<6} {'kd':<6} {'RMS':<12} {'Max':<12} {'Min':<12} {'Period':<10}")
+    print(f"{'-'*80}")
+
+    success_count = 0
+    results = []
+
+    for filename in sorted(csv_files):
+        try:
+            file_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, filename)
+
+            # Read CSV file
+            df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
+
+            # Get column names
+            torque_col, target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, body_part)
+
+            # Check required columns
+            if torque_col not in df.columns:
+                print(f"Warning: torque column not found in file '{file_path}': {torque_col}")
+                continue
+            if target_col not in df.columns:
+                print(f"Warning: target column not found in file '{file_path}': {target_col}")
+                continue
+
+            # Get data
+            torque_data = df[torque_col].dropna().values
+            target_data = df[target_col].dropna().values
+
+            # Find one complete period index range
+            try:
+                start_idx, end_idx = find_complete_period(target_data)
+            except ValueError as e:
+                print(f"Warning: file '{filename}' does not contain a complete period: {str(e)}")
+                continue
+
+            # Extract torque data within the period
+            period_torque = torque_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1]
+
+            # Compute RMS (root mean square)
+            # RMS = sqrt(mean(torque^2))
+            rms = np.sqrt(np.mean(period_torque**2))
+
+            # Compute max and min
+            torque_max = np.max(period_torque)
+            torque_min = np.min(period_torque)
+
+            # Compute period duration (0.002s sampling interval)
+            period_time = len(period_torque) * 0.002
+
+            # Extract PD parameter info
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(filename)
+            if params:
+                data_type, kp, kd, tag = params
+            else:
+                kp, kd = "N/A", "N/A"
+
+            # Print result line
+            result_line = f"{filename[:43]:<45} {kp:<6} {kd:<6} {rms:<12.6f} {torque_max:<12.6f} {torque_min:<12.6f} {period_time:<10.3f}"
+            print(result_line)
+            output_lines.append(result_line)
+            results.append(
+                {
+                    'filename': filename,
+                    'kp': kp,
+                    'kd': kd,
+                    'rms': rms,
+                    'max': torque_max,
+                    'min': torque_min,
+                    'period_time': period_time,
+                }
+            )
+
+            success_count += 1
+
+        except Exception as e:
+            error_msg = f"Warning: error occurred while processing file '{filename}': {str(e)}"
+            print(error_msg)
+            output_lines.append(error_msg)
+            continue
+
+    # Print summary
+    summary_line = f"{'-'*80}"
+    success_line = f"\nSuccessfully processed {success_count} files"
+    end_line = f"{'='*80}\n"
+
+    print(summary_line)
+    print(success_line)
+    print(end_line)
+
+    output_lines.append(summary_line)
+    output_lines.append(success_line)
+    output_lines.append(end_line)
+
+    # Save to text file
+    if output_to_file and success_count > 0:
+        output_file = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, f'torque_rms_joint_{joint_index}.txt')
+        with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
+            f.write('\n'.join(output_lines))
+        print(f"Results saved to: {output_file}")
+
+    return success_count > 0
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Compute RMS, max and min torque over a complete period.')
+    parser.add_argument(
+        'data_path',
+        type=parse_data_path,
+        help='Data root path (all joint_{number} folders under this path will be scanned).',
+        default='./data',
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        '--body-part',
+        choices=['left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist'],
+        default=None,
+        help='Body part (if provided, interactive selection is skipped).',
+    )
+
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    # Find all joint folders
+    joint_folders = find_joint_folders(args.data_path)
+
+    if not joint_folders:
+        print(f"Error: no folders with format 'joint_{{number}}' found under path '{args.data_path}'")
+        sys.exit(1)
+
+    print(f"\nFound {len(joint_folders)} joint folders under path '{args.data_path}':")
+    for folder_path, joint_idx in joint_folders:
+        print(f"  - {os.path.basename(folder_path)} (joint_{joint_idx})")
+
+    # Select body part (all joints share the same selection)
+    if args.body_part:
+        body_part = args.body_part
+        print(f"\nUsing body part specified via command line: {body_part}")
+    else:
+        body_part = select_body_part()
+        print(f"\nSelected body part: {body_part}")
+    print(f"Total joint folders to process: {len(joint_folders)}\n")
+
+    # Process each joint folder
+    total_success = 0
+    for folder_path, joint_index in joint_folders:
+        print(f"\nProcessing: {os.path.basename(folder_path)}")
+        success = compute_torque_rms_for_files(folder_path, joint_index, body_part, output_to_file=True)
+        if success:
+            total_success += 1
+
+    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+    print(f"All done: successfully processed {total_success}/{len(joint_folders)} joint folders")
+    print(f"{'='*80}\n")
+
+    if total_success == 0:
+        print("All processing failed!")
+        sys.exit(1)

+import pandas as pd
+import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
+import sys
+import argparse
+import os
+import re
+import numpy as np
+from scipy.signal import find_peaks
+from matplotlib.backends.backend_pdf import PdfPages
+
+
+def find_complete_period(target_data):
+    """
+    Find one complete period in the position (target) data.
+    Return the start and end indices of the period.
+    """
+    # Find all peak indices in target data
+    peaks, _ = find_peaks(target_data, distance=1)  # distance parameter can be tuned for different data
+
+    if len(peaks) < 3:
+        # If not enough peaks are found, we cannot determine a complete period
+        raise ValueError("Cannot find a complete period in the data")
+
+    # Return the start and end indices of the first complete period
+    return peaks[1], peaks[2]
+
+
+def extract_joint_number(folder_name):
+    """
+    Extract the joint index from a folder name.
+
+    Args:
+        folder_name: folder name in the format 'joint_{number}'.
+
+    Returns:
+        int: joint index or None if the format does not match.
+    """
+    pattern = r'joint_(\d+)'
+    match = re.match(pattern, folder_name)
+
+    if match:
+        return int(match.group(1))
+    else:
+        return None
+
+
+def extract_parameters_from_filename(filename):
+    """
+    Extract parameter information and tag from a file name.
+
+    Args:
+        filename: file name, format '{sim/real}_p_{kp}_d_{kd}...' (extra suffix is allowed).
+
+    Returns:
+        tuple: (data_type, kp, kd, tag) or None if the format does not match.
+    """
+    pattern = r'^(sim|real)_p_(\d+)_d_(\d+)(.*)'
+    match = re.match(pattern, filename)
+
+    if match:
+        data_type = match.group(1)  # 'sim' or 'real'
+        kp = int(match.group(2))
+        kd = int(match.group(3))
+        tag = match.group(4).strip()  # extract tag (remove leading/trailing spaces)
+        return data_type, kp, kd, tag
+    else:
+        return None
+
+
+def select_body_part():
+    """
+    Interactively select a body part.
+
+    Returns:
+        str: selected body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
+    print("Please select the body part corresponding to the data:")
+    print("=" * 60)
+    print("1. Left leg  (left_leg)")
+    print("2. Right leg (right_leg)")
+    print("3. Left arm  (left_arm)")
+    print("4. Right arm (right_arm)")
+    print("5. Waist     (waist)")
+    print("=" * 60)
+
+    while True:
+        try:
+            choice = input("Please enter your choice (1-5): ").strip()
+            if choice == '1':
+                return 'left_leg'
+            elif choice == '2':
+                return 'right_leg'
+            elif choice == '3':
+                return 'left_arm'
+            elif choice == '4':
+                return 'right_arm'
+            elif choice == '5':
+                return 'waist'
+            else:
+                print("Invalid option, please enter a number between 1 and 5.")
+        except (EOFError, KeyboardInterrupt):
+            print("\n\nOperation cancelled.")
+            sys.exit(0)
+
+
+def get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, data_type, body_part):
+    """
+    Get position, velocity and target column names for a given joint index, data type and body part.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        data_type: 'sim' or 'real'.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+
+    Returns:
+        tuple: (position_column_name, velocity_column_name, target_column_name).
+    """
+    if data_type == 'sim':
+        if body_part == 'left_leg':
+            pos_col = f'leg_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index}'
+            vel_col = f'leg_joint_vel_gym_{joint_index}'
+            target_col = f'target_leg_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index}'
+        elif body_part == 'right_leg':
+            pos_col = f'leg_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index+6}'
+            vel_col = f'leg_joint_vel_gym_{joint_index+6}'
+            target_col = f'target_leg_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index+6}'
+        elif body_part == 'left_arm':
+            pos_col = f'arm_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+            vel_col = f'arm_joint_vel_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+            target_col = f'target_arm_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+        elif body_part == 'right_arm':
+            pos_col = f'arm_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+            vel_col = f'arm_joint_vel_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+            target_col = f'target_arm_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index + 7}'
+        elif body_part == 'waist':
+            pos_col = f'waist_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index}'
+            vel_col = f'waist_joint_vel_gym_{joint_index}'
+            target_col = f'target_waist_joint_pos_gym_{joint_index}'
+        else:
+            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported body part: {body_part}")
+    elif data_type == 'real':
+        if body_part == 'left_leg':
+            pos_col = f'/joint_state/leg_l_joint_state_open_chain/position[{joint_index}]'
+            vel_col = f'/joint_state/leg_l_joint_state_open_chain/velocity[{joint_index}]'
+            target_col = f'/leg_joint_control_test/leg_l_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+        elif body_part == 'right_leg':
+            pos_col = f'/joint_state/leg_r_joint_state_open_chain/position[{joint_index}]'
+            vel_col = f'/joint_state/leg_r_joint_state_open_chain/velocity[{joint_index}]'
+            target_col = f'/leg_joint_control_test/leg_r_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+        elif body_part == 'left_arm':
+            pos_col = f'/joint_state/arm_l_joint_state_open_chain/position[{joint_index}]'
+            vel_col = f'/joint_state/arm_l_joint_state_open_chain/velocity[{joint_index}]'
+            target_col = f'/arm_test/arm_l_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+        elif body_part == 'right_arm':
+            pos_col = f'/joint_state/arm_r_joint_state_open_chain/position[{joint_index}]'
+            vel_col = f'/joint_state/arm_r_joint_state_open_chain/velocity[{joint_index}]'
+            target_col = f'/arm_test/arm_r_joint_target/position[{joint_index}]'
+        elif body_part == 'waist':
+            pos_col = f'/joint_state/waist_joint_state_open_chain/position[{joint_index}]'
+            vel_col = f'/joint_state/waist_joint_state_open_chain/velocity[{joint_index}]'
+            target_col = f'/waist_test/waist_joint_target_.position[{joint_index}]'
+        else:
+            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported body part: {body_part}")
+    else:
+        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported data type: {data_type}")
+
+    return pos_col, vel_col, target_col

+def plot_combined_diagrams_for_pd_params(joint_folder_path, joint_index, kp, kd, output_folder, body_part):
+    """
+    Plot phase diagram and single-period velocity curves for given PD parameters,
+    including comparison between simulation and real data.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        kp: proportional gain.
+        kd: derivative gain.
+        output_folder: output folder path.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    # Create subplots
+    fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(20, 8))
+
+    # Find corresponding sim and real files (file names may contain tags)
+    sim_pattern = f'sim_p_{kp}_d_{kd}'
+    real_pattern = f'real_p_{kp}_d_{kd}'
+
+    # Get all CSV files
+    csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(joint_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+
+    # Find matching files
+    sim_files = [f for f in csv_files if f.startswith(sim_pattern)]
+    real_files = [f for f in csv_files if f.startswith(real_pattern)]
+
+    # Define colors and markers
+    sim_color = 'b'  # blue for simulation
+    sim_marker = 'o'
+    # Define a set of colors and markers for real files
+    real_colors = ['r', 'g', 'm', 'orange', 'purple', 'brown', 'pink', 'olive', 'cyan', 'yellow']
+    real_markers = ['s', '^', 'v', 'D', 'p', '*', 'h', 'X', '+', 'x']  # different markers for better distinction
+
+    data_found = False
+
+    # Process sim files
+    for sim_file in sim_files:
+        try:
+            file_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, sim_file)
+
+            # Read CSV file
+            df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
+
+            # Get column names
+            pos_col, vel_col, target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'sim', body_part)
+
+            # Check required columns
+            if pos_col not in df.columns or vel_col not in df.columns:
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in file '{file_path}'")
+                print(f"Position column '{pos_col}' or velocity column '{vel_col}' does not exist")
+                continue
+
+            # Extract tag info
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(sim_file)
+            tag = params[3] if params else ""
+            label = f"Simulation (kp={kp}, kd={kd})"
+            if tag:
+                label += f", tag={tag}"
+
+            # Get non-NaN position, velocity and target data
+            position_data = df[pos_col].dropna().values
+            velocity_data = df[vel_col].dropna().values
+            target_data = df[target_col].dropna().values
+
+            # Plot phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.plot(
+                position_data,
+                velocity_data,
+                color=sim_color,
+                marker=sim_marker,
+                linestyle='none',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=label,
+                markersize=3,
+            )
+
+            # Plot single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            try:
+                # Find one complete period based on target data
+                start_idx, end_idx = find_complete_period(target_data)
+
+                # Generate time series (0.002s sampling interval)
+                time = np.arange(len(velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+
+                ax2.plot(time, velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1], color=sim_color, label=label, linewidth=2)
+
+                # Print period information
+                period_time = len(velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1]) * 0.002
+                print(f"Period duration for file '{file_path}': {period_time:.3f}s")
+
+            except ValueError as e:
+                print(f"Warning: could not find a complete period in file '{file_path}': {str(e)}")
+                # If no complete period is found, plot full velocity curve
+                time = np.arange(len(velocity_data)) * 0.002
+                ax2.plot(time, velocity_data, color=sim_color, label=f"{label} (full)", linewidth=2)
+
+            # Compute target statistics (only for the first sim file)
+            if not data_found and target_col in df.columns:
+                target_data = df[target_col].dropna().values
+                target_min = np.min(target_data)
+                target_max = np.max(target_data)
+                target_amplitude_rad = (target_max - target_min) / 2.0
+                target_amplitude_deg = target_amplitude_rad * 180.0 / np.pi
+                target_mean = (target_max + target_min) / 2.0
+                print(
+                    f"  Sim Target - Min: {target_min:.6f} rad, Max: {target_max:.6f} rad, "
+                    f"Amplitude: {target_amplitude_deg:.6f} deg, Mean: {target_mean:.6f} rad"
+                )
+
+            data_found = True
+            print(f"Successfully loaded sim data: {file_path}")
+
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Warning: error occurred while processing file '{file_path}': {str(e)}")
+
+    # Process real files (use different colors for different files)
+    for idx, real_file in enumerate(real_files):
+        try:
+            file_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, real_file)
+
+            # Read CSV file
+            df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
+
+            # Get column names
+            pos_col, vel_col, target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'real', body_part)
+
+            # Check required columns
+            if pos_col not in df.columns or vel_col not in df.columns:
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in file '{file_path}'")
+                print(f"Position column '{pos_col}' or velocity column '{vel_col}' does not exist")
+                continue
+
+            # Extract tag info
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(real_file)
+            tag = params[3] if params else ""
+            label = f"Real (kp={kp}, kd={kd})"
+            if tag:
+                label += f", tag={tag}"
+            # If there are multiple real files, add an index to the label
+            if len(real_files) > 1:
+                label += f" (#{idx+1})"
+
+            # Select color and marker (cycle through lists)
+            real_color = real_colors[idx % len(real_colors)]
+            real_marker = real_markers[idx % len(real_markers)]
+
+            # Get non-NaN position, velocity and target data
+            position_data = df[pos_col].dropna().values
+            velocity_data = df[vel_col].dropna().values
+            target_data = df[target_col].dropna().values
+
+            # Plot phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.plot(
+                position_data,
+                velocity_data,
+                color=real_color,
+                marker=real_marker,
+                linestyle='none',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=label,
+                markersize=3,
+            )
+
+            # Plot single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            try:
+                # Find one complete period based on target data
+                start_idx, end_idx = find_complete_period(target_data)
+
+                # Generate time series (0.002s sampling interval)
+                time = np.arange(len(velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+
+                ax2.plot(time, velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1], color=real_color, label=label, linewidth=2)
+
+                # Print period information
+                period_time = len(velocity_data[start_idx : end_idx + 1]) * 0.002
+                print(f"Period duration for file '{file_path}': {period_time:.3f}s")
+
+            except ValueError as e:
+                print(f"Warning: could not find a complete period in file '{file_path}': {str(e)}")
+                # If no complete period is found, plot full velocity curve
+                time = np.arange(len(velocity_data)) * 0.002
+                ax2.plot(time, velocity_data, color=real_color, label=f"{label} (full)", linewidth=2)
+
+            # Compute target statistics (only for the first real file)
+            if idx == 0 and target_col in df.columns:
+                target_data = df[target_col].dropna().values
+                target_min = np.min(target_data)
+                target_max = np.max(target_data)
+                target_amplitude_rad = (target_max - target_min) / 2.0
+                target_amplitude_deg = target_amplitude_rad * 180.0 / np.pi
+                target_mean = (target_max + target_min) / 2.0
+                print(
+                    f"  Real Target - Min: {target_min:.6f} rad, Max: {target_max:.6f} rad, "
+                    f"Amplitude: {target_amplitude_deg:.6f} deg, Mean: {target_mean:.6f} rad"
+                )
+
+            data_found = True
+            print(f"Successfully loaded real data: {file_path} (color: {real_color})")
+
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Warning: error occurred while processing file '{file_path}': {str(e)}")
+
+    if not data_found:
+        print(f"Error: no valid data files found for PD parameters (kp={kp}, kd={kd})")
+        plt.close()
+        return False
+
+    # Configure phase diagram (left subplot)
+    ax1.set_xlabel('q (rad)')
+    ax1.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+    ax1.set_title(f'Phase Diagram - Joint {joint_index} (kp={kp}, kd={kd})')
+    ax1.legend()
+    ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+    # Configure single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+    ax2.set_xlabel('t (s)')
+    ax2.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+    ax2.set_title(f'Single Period Velocity - Joint {joint_index} (kp={kp}, kd={kd})')
+    ax2.legend()
+    ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+    # Adjust layout
+    plt.tight_layout()
+
+    # Ensure output folder exists
+    os.makedirs(output_folder, exist_ok=True)
+
+    # Save figure
+    output_file = os.path.join(output_folder, f'combined_diagrams_joint_{joint_index}_p_{kp}_d_{kd}.png')
+    plt.savefig(output_file, dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
+    print(f"Combined figure saved to: {output_file}")
+
+    # Close figure to release memory
+    plt.close()
+
+    return True
+
+
+def plot_compare_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part):
+    """
+    Plot comparison figures for all CSV files under the 'compare' subfolder of a joint folder.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        output_folder: output folder path.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    # Real data folder
+    real_folder_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, 'compare', 'real')
+    if not os.path.exists(real_folder_path):
+        print(f"Error: compare real folder does not exist: {real_folder_path}")
+        return False
+
+    # Get all CSV files in compare/real
+    real_csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(real_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not real_csv_files:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files found in compare real folder '{real_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Sim data folder
+    sim_folder_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, 'compare', 'sim')
+    if not os.path.exists(sim_folder_path):
+        print(f"Error: compare sim folder does not exist: {sim_folder_path}")
+        return False
+
+    # Get all CSV files in compare/sim
+    sim_csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(sim_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not sim_csv_files:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files found in compare sim folder '{sim_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Ensure output folder exists
+    os.makedirs(output_folder, exist_ok=True)
+
+    # PDF output file
+    output_file = os.path.join(output_folder, f'compare_combined_diagrams_joint_{joint_index}.pdf')
+
+    # joint_pos_center = [0.0, 0.0, -0.481, 0.907, -0.398, 0.0]  # for leg joint
+    # joint_pos_center = [0.0, 0.174, 0.174, 0.0, 0.0]  # for waist joint
+    joint_pos_center = [0.0, 0.174, 0.0, 0.348, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0]
+    pos_min = joint_pos_center[joint_index] - 0.4
+    pos_max = joint_pos_center[joint_index] + 0.4
+    vel_min = -2.0
+    vel_max = 2.0
+
+    with PdfPages(output_file) as pdf:
+
+        for idx, filename in enumerate(sorted(real_csv_files)):
+            print(f'Reading file: {filename}')
+            # Extract PD parameters
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(filename)
+            if not params:
+                print(f"Warning: file '{filename}' does not match the expected name pattern, skip")
+                continue
+
+            _, real_kp, real_kd, _ = params
+            real_file_path = os.path.join(real_folder_path, filename)
+
+            selected_sim_file_path = None
+            for sim_filename in sim_csv_files:
+                params = extract_parameters_from_filename(sim_filename)
+                if not params:
+                    print(f"Warning: file '{sim_filename}' does not match the expected name pattern, skip")
+                    continue
+
+                _, sim_kp, sim_kd, _ = params
+                if sim_kp == real_kp and sim_kd == real_kd:
+                    selected_sim_file_path = os.path.join(sim_folder_path, sim_filename)
+                    print(f'Matched sim file: {selected_sim_file_path}')
+                    break
+
+            # Create subplots
+            fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(20, 8))
+
+            # Read CSV files
+            real_df = pd.read_csv(real_file_path)
+            sim_df = pd.read_csv(selected_sim_file_path)
+
+            # Check required columns
+            real_pos_col, real_vel_col, real_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'real', body_part)
+            if (
+                real_pos_col not in real_df.columns
+                or real_vel_col not in real_df.columns
+                or real_target_col not in real_df.columns
+            ):
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in real file '{real_file_path}'")
+                continue
+            sim_pos_col, sim_vel_col, sim_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'sim', body_part)
+            if (
+                sim_pos_col not in sim_df.columns
+                or sim_vel_col not in sim_df.columns
+                or sim_target_col not in sim_df.columns
+            ):
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in sim file '{selected_sim_file_path}'")
+                continue
+
+            # Get non-NaN position, velocity and target data
+            real_position_data = real_df[real_pos_col].dropna().values
+            real_velocity_data = real_df[real_vel_col].dropna().values
+            real_target_data = real_df[real_target_col].dropna().values
+            sim_position_data = sim_df[sim_pos_col].dropna().values
+            sim_velocity_data = sim_df[sim_vel_col].dropna().values
+            sim_target_data = sim_df[sim_target_col].dropna().values
+            # Plot phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.plot(
+                real_position_data,
+                real_velocity_data,
+                color='r',
+                linestyle='-',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=f'real (kp={real_kp}, kd={real_kd})',
+                # markersize=3,
+            )
+            ax1.plot(
+                sim_position_data,
+                sim_velocity_data,
+                color='b',
+                linestyle='--',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=f'sim (kp={sim_kp}, kd={sim_kd})',
+                # markersize=3,
+            )
+
+            # Plot single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            real_start_idx, real_end_idx = find_complete_period(real_target_data)
+            sim_start_idx, sim_end_idx = find_complete_period(sim_target_data)
+            print(f"real_start_idx: {real_start_idx}, real_end_idx: {real_end_idx}")
+            print(f"sim_start_idx: {sim_start_idx}, sim_end_idx: {sim_end_idx}")
+
+            # Generate time series (0.002s sampling interval)
+            real_time = np.arange(len(real_velocity_data[real_start_idx : real_end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+            sim_time = np.arange(len(sim_velocity_data[sim_start_idx : sim_end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+
+            ax2.plot(
+                real_time,
+                real_velocity_data[real_start_idx : real_end_idx + 1],
+                color='r',
+                linestyle='-',
+                label=f'real (kp={real_kp}, kd={real_kd})',
+                linewidth=2,
+            )
+            # ax2.plot(
+            #     real_time,
+            #     real_target_data[real_start_idx : real_end_idx + 1],
+            #     color='r',
+            #     linestyle=':',
+            #     label=f'real target',
+            #     linewidth=2,
+            #     alpha=0.3,
+            # )
+
+            ax2.plot(
+                sim_time,
+                sim_velocity_data[sim_start_idx : sim_end_idx + 1],
+                color='b',
+                linestyle='--',
+                label=f'sim (kp={real_kp}, kd={real_kd})',
+                linewidth=2,
+            )
+            # ax2.plot(
+            #     sim_time,
+            #     sim_target_data[sim_start_idx : sim_end_idx + 1],
+            #     color='b',
+            #     linestyle='-.',
+            #     label=f'sim target',
+            #     linewidth=2,
+            #     alpha=0.3,
+            # )
+
+            print(f"Successfully loaded data: {filename}")
+
+            # Configure phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.set_xlabel('q (rad)')
+            ax1.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+            ax1.set_title(f'Compare Folder Phase Diagram - Joint {joint_index}')
+
+            # Set axis limits
+            ax1.set_xlim(pos_min, pos_max)
+            ax1.set_ylim(vel_min, vel_max)
+            ax1.legend(bbox_to_anchor=(1.05, 1), loc='upper left', fontsize=8)
+            ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+            # Configure single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            ax2.set_xlabel('t (s)')
+            ax2.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+            ax2.set_title(f'Compare Folder Single Period Velocity - Joint {joint_index}')
+            ax2.legend(bbox_to_anchor=(1.05, 1), loc='upper left', fontsize=8)
+            ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+            # Adjust layout
+            plt.tight_layout()
+
+            pdf.savefig(fig, bbox_inches='tight', dpi=300)
+            plt.close()
+
+    return True
+
+
+def plot_target_position_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part):
+    """
+    Compute amplitude (in degrees) and mean of sim and real target position curves
+    in a joint folder. The target is a sine signal; statistics are computed using
+    its maximum and minimum values.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        output_folder: output folder path (kept for API compatibility, not used).
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    # Get all CSV files in joint folder
+    csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(joint_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not csv_files:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files found in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Separate sim and real files
+    sim_files = [f for f in csv_files if f.startswith('sim_')]
+    real_files = [f for f in csv_files if f.startswith('real_')]
+
+    if not sim_files:
+        print(f"Error: no sim files found in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    if not real_files:
+        print(f"Error: no real files found in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Collect all unique PD parameter pairs (kp, kd), ignore tag
+    pd_params = set()
+    for filename in csv_files:
+        params = extract_parameters_from_filename(filename)
+        if params:
+            data_type, kp, kd, tag = params
+            # Only use kp and kd as identifier, ignore tag
+            pd_params.add((kp, kd))
+
+    if not pd_params:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files with the expected naming pattern in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+    print(f"Joint {joint_index} - Target Position Statistics")
+    print(f"{'='*80}")
+    print(f"{'kp':<8} {'kd':<8} {'Type':<8} {'Min':<12} {'Max':<12} {'Amplitude(deg)':<15} {'Mean':<12}")
+    print(f"{'-'*80}")
+
+    success_count = 0
+
+    for kp, kd in sorted(pd_params):
+        # Find matching sim and real files
+        sim_pattern = f'sim_p_{kp}_d_{kd}'
+        real_pattern = f'real_p_{kp}_d_{kd}'
+
+        matching_sim_files = [f for f in sim_files if f.startswith(sim_pattern)]
+        matching_real_files = [f for f in real_files if f.startswith(real_pattern)]
+
+        if not matching_sim_files:
+            print(f"Warning: no matching sim files found (kp={kp}, kd={kd})")
+            continue
+
+        if not matching_real_files:
+            print(f"Warning: no matching real files found (kp={kp}, kd={kd})")
+            continue
+
+        # Use the first matching file for each type
+        sim_filename = matching_sim_files[0]
+        real_filename = matching_real_files[0]
+
+        sim_file_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, sim_filename)
+        real_file_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, real_filename)
+
+        # Read CSV files
+        try:
+            real_df = pd.read_csv(real_file_path)
+            sim_df = pd.read_csv(sim_file_path)
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"Warning: failed to read CSV files: {str(e)}")
+            continue
+
+        # Check required columns
+        real_pos_col, real_vel_col, real_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'real', body_part)
+        if real_target_col not in real_df.columns:
+            print(f"Warning: target column not found in real file '{real_file_path}': {real_target_col}")
+            continue
+        sim_pos_col, sim_vel_col, sim_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'sim', body_part)
+        if sim_target_col not in sim_df.columns:
+            print(f"Warning: target column not found in sim file '{sim_file_path}': {sim_target_col}")
+            continue
+
+        # Get target position data
+        real_target_data = real_df[real_target_col].dropna().values
+        sim_target_data = sim_df[sim_target_col].dropna().values
+
+        # Compute statistics for real target
+        real_min = np.min(real_target_data)
+        real_max = np.max(real_target_data)
+        real_amplitude_rad = (real_max - real_min) / 2.0
+        real_amplitude_deg = real_amplitude_rad * 180.0 / np.pi  # convert to degrees
+        real_mean = (real_max + real_min) / 2.0
+
+        # Compute statistics for sim target
+        sim_min = np.min(sim_target_data)
+        sim_max = np.max(sim_target_data)
+        sim_amplitude_rad = (sim_max - sim_min) / 2.0
+        sim_amplitude_deg = sim_amplitude_rad * 180.0 / np.pi  # convert to degrees
+        sim_mean = (sim_max + sim_min) / 2.0
+
+        # Print results
+        print(
+            f"{kp:<8} {kd:<8} {'real':<8} {real_min:<12.6f} {real_max:<12.6f} {real_amplitude_deg:<15.6f} {real_mean:<12.6f}"
+        )
+        print(
+            f"{kp:<8} {kd:<8} {'sim':<8} {sim_min:<12.6f} {sim_max:<12.6f} {sim_amplitude_deg:<15.6f} {sim_mean:<12.6f}"
+        )
+
+        # Compute differences
+        amplitude_diff = abs(real_amplitude_deg - sim_amplitude_deg)
+        mean_diff = abs(real_mean - sim_mean)
+        print(f"{'':<8} {'':<8} {'diff':<8} {'':<12} {'':<12} {amplitude_diff:<15.6f} {mean_diff:<12.6f}")
+        print(f"{'-'*80}")
+
+        success_count += 1
+
+    print(f"\nSuccessfully processed {success_count} PD parameter combinations")
+    print(f"{'='*80}\n")
+
+    return success_count > 0
+
+
+def plot_left_and_right_leg_compare_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part):
+    """
+    Plot comparison figures for all CSV files under the left/right compare subfolders
+    of a joint folder.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        joint_index: joint index.
+        output_folder: output folder path.
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+    """
+    # Left leg folder
+    left_folder_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, 'compare', 'left')
+    if not os.path.exists(left_folder_path):
+        print(f"Error: compare left folder does not exist: {left_folder_path}")
+        return False
+
+    # Get all CSV files in compare/left
+    left_csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(left_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not left_csv_files:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files found in compare left folder '{left_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Right leg folder
+    right_folder_path = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, 'compare', 'right')
+    if not os.path.exists(right_folder_path):
+        print(f"Error: compare right folder does not exist: {right_folder_path}")
+        return False
+
+    # Get all CSV files in compare/right
+    right_csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(right_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+    if not right_csv_files:
+        print(f"Error: no CSV files found in compare right folder '{right_folder_path}'")
+        return False
+
+    # Ensure output folder exists
+    os.makedirs(output_folder, exist_ok=True)
+
+    # PDF output file
+    output_file = os.path.join(output_folder, f'compare_left_and_right_leg_joint_{joint_index}.pdf')
+
+    joint_pos_center = [0.0, 0.0, -0.481, 0.907, -0.398, 0.0]  # for leg joint
+    # joint_pos_center = [0.0, 0.174, 0.174, 0.0, 0.0]  # for waist joint
+    pos_min = joint_pos_center[joint_index] - 0.4
+    pos_max = joint_pos_center[joint_index] + 0.4
+    vel_min = -2.0
+    vel_max = 2.0
+
+    with PdfPages(output_file) as pdf:
+
+        for idx, filename in enumerate(sorted(left_csv_files)):
+            print(f"Reading file: {filename}")
+            # Extract PD parameters
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(filename)
+            if not params:
+                print(f"Warning: file '{filename}' does not match the expected name pattern, skip")
+                continue
+
+            _, left_kp, left_kd, _ = params
+            left_file_path = os.path.join(left_folder_path, filename)
+
+            selected_right_file_path = None
+            for right_filename in right_csv_files:
+                params = extract_parameters_from_filename(right_filename)
+                if not params:
+                    print(f"Warning: file '{right_filename}' does not match the expected name pattern, skip")
+                    continue
+
+                _, right_kp, right_kd, _ = params
+                if right_kp == left_kp and right_kd == left_kd:
+                    selected_right_file_path = os.path.join(right_folder_path, right_filename)
+                    print(f'Matched right file: {selected_right_file_path}')
+                    break
+
+            # Create subplots
+            fig, (ax1, ax2) = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(20, 8))
+
+            # Read CSV files
+            left_df = pd.read_csv(left_file_path)
+            right_df = pd.read_csv(selected_right_file_path)
+
+            # Check required columns
+            left_pos_col, left_vel_col, left_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(joint_index, 'real', 'left_leg')
+            if (
+                left_pos_col not in left_df.columns
+                or left_vel_col not in left_df.columns
+                or left_target_col not in left_df.columns
+            ):
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in left file '{left_file_path}'")
+                continue
+            right_pos_col, right_vel_col, right_target_col = get_column_names_for_joint(
+                joint_index, 'real', 'right_leg'
+            )
+            if (
+                right_pos_col not in right_df.columns
+                or right_vel_col not in right_df.columns
+                or right_target_col not in right_df.columns
+            ):
+                print(f"Warning: required columns not found in right file '{selected_right_file_path}'")
+                continue
+
+            # Get non-NaN position, velocity and target data
+            left_position_data = left_df[left_pos_col].dropna().values
+            left_velocity_data = left_df[left_vel_col].dropna().values
+            left_target_data = left_df[left_target_col].dropna().values
+            right_position_data = right_df[right_pos_col].dropna().values
+            right_velocity_data = right_df[right_vel_col].dropna().values
+            right_target_data = right_df[right_target_col].dropna().values
+            # Plot phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.plot(
+                left_position_data,
+                left_velocity_data,
+                color='r',
+                linestyle='-',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=f'left (kp={left_kp}, kd={left_kd})',
+                # markersize=3,
+            )
+            ax1.plot(
+                right_position_data,
+                right_velocity_data,
+                color='b',
+                linestyle='--',
+                alpha=0.6,
+                label=f'right (kp={right_kp}, kd={right_kd})',
+                # markersize=3,
+            )
+
+            # Plot single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            left_start_idx, left_end_idx = find_complete_period(left_target_data)
+            right_start_idx, right_end_idx = find_complete_period(right_target_data)
+            print(f"left_start_idx: {left_start_idx}, left_end_idx: {left_end_idx}")
+            print(f"right_start_idx: {right_start_idx}, right_end_idx: {right_end_idx}")
+
+            # Generate time series (0.002s sampling interval)
+            left_time = np.arange(len(left_velocity_data[left_start_idx : left_end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+            right_time = np.arange(len(right_velocity_data[right_start_idx : right_end_idx + 1])) * 0.002
+
+            ax2.plot(
+                left_time,
+                left_velocity_data[left_start_idx : left_end_idx + 1],
+                color='r',
+                linestyle='-',
+                label=f'left (kp={left_kp}, kd={left_kd})',
+                linewidth=2,
+            )
+            # ax2.plot(
+            #     left_time,
+            #     left_target_data[left_start_idx : left_end_idx + 1],
+            #     color='r',
+            #     linestyle=':',
+            #     label=f'left target',
+            #     linewidth=2,
+            #     alpha=0.3,
+            # )
+
+            ax2.plot(
+                right_time,
+                right_velocity_data[right_start_idx : right_end_idx + 1],
+                color='b',
+                linestyle='--',
+                label=f'right (kp={left_kp}, kd={left_kd})',
+                linewidth=2,
+            )
+            # ax2.plot(
+            #     right_time,
+            #     right_target_data[right_start_idx : right_end_idx + 1],
+            #     color='b',
+            #     linestyle='-.',
+            #     label=f'right target',
+            #     linewidth=2,
+            #     alpha=0.3,
+            # )
+
+            print(f"Successfully loaded data: {filename}")
+
+            # Configure phase diagram (left subplot)
+            ax1.set_xlabel('q (rad)')
+            ax1.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+            ax1.set_title(f'Compare Folder Phase Diagram - Joint {joint_index}')
+
+            # Set axis limits
+            ax1.set_xlim(pos_min, pos_max)
+            ax1.set_ylim(vel_min, vel_max)
+            ax1.legend(bbox_to_anchor=(1.05, 1), loc='upper left', fontsize=8)
+            ax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+            # Configure single-period velocity curve (right subplot)
+            ax2.set_xlabel('t (s)')
+            ax2.set_ylabel('dq (rad/s)')
+            ax2.set_title(f'Compare Folder Single Period Velocity - Joint {joint_index}')
+            ax2.legend(bbox_to_anchor=(1.05, 1), loc='upper left', fontsize=8)
+            ax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
+
+            # Adjust layout
+            plt.tight_layout()
+
+            pdf.savefig(fig, bbox_inches='tight', dpi=300)
+            plt.close()
+
+    return True
+
+
+def process_joint_folder(joint_folder_path, plot_mode='individual', body_part='left_leg'):
+    """
+    Process a single joint folder and plot figures according to the mode.
+
+    Args:
+        joint_folder_path: joint folder path.
+        plot_mode: plot mode ('individual', 'compare', 'left_right_compare', 'target_compare').
+        body_part: body part ('left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist').
+
+    Returns:
+        bool: True if at least one figure is generated successfully.
+    """
+    # Extract joint index from folder name
+    folder_name = os.path.basename(joint_folder_path)
+    joint_index = extract_joint_number(folder_name)
+
+    if joint_index is None:
+        print(f"Error: folder name '{folder_name}' does not match format 'joint_{{number}}'")
+        return False
+
+    print(f"\nProcessing joint folder: {folder_name}")
+    print(f"Joint index: {joint_index}")
+    print(f"Plot mode: {plot_mode}")
+
+    # Create output folder
+    output_folder = os.path.join(joint_folder_path, 'phase')
+
+    success_count = 0
+
+    if plot_mode == 'individual':
+        # Get all CSV files
+        csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(joint_folder_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
+
+        if not csv_files:
+            print(f"Error: no CSV files found in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+            return False
+
+        # Collect all unique PD parameter pairs (kp, kd), ignore tag.
+        # plot_combined_diagrams_for_pd_params will find all matching files (including different tags).
+        pd_params = set()
+        for filename in csv_files:
+            params = extract_parameters_from_filename(filename)
+            if params:
+                data_type, kp, kd, tag = params
+                # Only use kp and kd as identifier, ignore tag
+                pd_params.add((kp, kd))
+
+        if not pd_params:
+            print(f"Error: no CSV files with the expected naming pattern in folder '{joint_folder_path}'")
+            return False
+
+        print(f"Found {len(pd_params)} PD parameter combinations.")
+
+        # Plot combined figures for each PD parameter pair
+        for kp, kd in sorted(pd_params):
+            print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+            print(f"Processing PD parameters: kp={kp}, kd={kd}")
+            print(f"{'='*80}")
+            try:
+                success = plot_combined_diagrams_for_pd_params(
+                    joint_folder_path, joint_index, kp, kd, output_folder, body_part
+                )
+                if success:
+                    success_count += 1
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"Error while processing PD parameters (kp={kp}, kd={kd}): {str(e)}")
+
+    elif plot_mode == 'compare':
+        print(f"\nPlotting comparison figures for 'compare' folder...")
+        success = plot_compare_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part)
+        if success:
+            success_count += 1
+    elif plot_mode == 'left_right_compare':
+        print(f"\nPlotting comparison figures for left and right leg folders...")
+        success = plot_left_and_right_leg_compare_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part)
+        if success:
+            success_count += 1
+    elif plot_mode == 'target_compare':
+        print(f"\nComputing target position statistics...")
+        success = plot_target_position_comparison(joint_folder_path, joint_index, output_folder, body_part)
+        if success:
+            success_count += 1
+
+    print(f"\nJoint {joint_index} processing finished!")
+    print(f"Successfully generated {success_count} figures/statistics.")
+
+    return success_count > 0
+
+
+def parse_data_path(arg):
+    """Parse and validate the data path argument."""
+    if not os.path.isdir(arg):
+        raise argparse.ArgumentTypeError(f"Path does not exist: '{arg}'")
+    return arg
+
+
+def find_joint_folders(data_path):
+    """
+    Find all folders in the given path that match the pattern 'joint_{number}'.
+
+    Args:
+        data_path: root data path.
+
+    Returns:
+        list: list of tuples (folder_path, joint_index).
+    """
+    joint_folders = []
+    for item in os.listdir(data_path):
+        item_path = os.path.join(data_path, item)
+        if os.path.isdir(item_path) and item.startswith('joint_'):
+            joint_index = extract_joint_number(item)
+            if joint_index is not None:
+                joint_folders.append((item_path, joint_index))
+
+    return sorted(joint_folders, key=lambda x: x[1])  # sort by joint index
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Plot phase diagrams and single-period velocity curves for joints.')
+    parser.add_argument(
+        'data_path',
+        type=parse_data_path,
+        help='Data root path (all joint_{number} folders under this path will be scanned).',
+        default='./data',
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        '--mode',
+        choices=['individual', 'compare', 'left_right_compare', 'target_compare'],
+        default='individual',
+        help=(
+            'Plot mode: '
+            'individual (compare sim vs real for the same PD parameters), '
+            'compare (compare all CSV files under compare folder), '
+            'left_right_compare (compare left and right legs), '
+            'target_compare (compare target position statistics)'
+        ),
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        '--body-part',
+        choices=['left_leg', 'right_leg', 'left_arm', 'right_arm', 'waist'],
+        default=None,
+        help='Body part (if provided, interactive selection is skipped).',
+    )
+
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    # Find all joint folders
+    joint_folders = find_joint_folders(args.data_path)
+
+    if not joint_folders:
+        print(f"Error: no folders with format 'joint_{{number}}' found under path '{args.data_path}'")
+        sys.exit(1)
+
+    print(f"\nFound {len(joint_folders)} joint folders under path '{args.data_path}':")
+    for folder_path, joint_idx in joint_folders:
+        print(f"  - {os.path.basename(folder_path)} (joint_{joint_idx})")
+    print(f"\nPlot mode: {args.mode}")
+
+    # Select body part (all joints share the same selection)
+    if args.body_part:
+        body_part = args.body_part
+        print(f"\nUsing body part specified via command line: {body_part}")
+    else:
+        body_part = select_body_part()
+        print(f"\nSelected body part: {body_part}")
+    print(f"Total joint folders to process: {len(joint_folders)}\n")
+
+    # Process each joint folder
+    total_success = 0
+    for folder_path, joint_index in joint_folders:
+        print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+        print(f"Processing: {os.path.basename(folder_path)}")
+        print(f"{'='*80}")
+        success = process_joint_folder(folder_path, args.mode, body_part)
+        if success:
+            total_success += 1
+
+    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
+    print(f"All done: successfully processed {total_success}/{len(joint_folders)} joint folders")
+    print(f"{'='*80}\n")
+
+    if total_success == 0:
+        print("All processing failed!")
+        sys.exit(1)

+package lcm_r01_v111;
+
+struct sim_t
+{
+    const int64_t DOF_WAIST = 3;
+    const int64_t DOF_NECK = 3;
+    const int64_t DOF_ARM = 14;
+    const int64_t DOF_LEG = 12;
+    const int64_t DOF_ALL = 32;
+    const int64_t DOF_JACOBIAN = 38;  // 6+DOF_ALL
+
+    int64_t counter;
+
+    double dof_state[DOF_ALL][2];
+
+    double pelvis_state[13];
+    double torso_state[13];
+    double head_state[13];
+    double hand_state[2][13];
+    double foot_state[2][13];
+
+    double hand_jacobian_wld[2][6][DOF_JACOBIAN];
+    double foot_jacobian_wld[2][6][DOF_JACOBIAN];
+
+    double hand_contact_force_wld[2][3];
+    double foot_contact_force_wld[2][3];
+}
+
+struct usr_t
+{
+    double joy_value[7];
+    boolean no_torque;
+    boolean reset;
+    double hand_tgt[2][6];
+    double j3_tgt[2];
+    double arm_pos_tgt[2][7];
+}
+
+struct ctl_t
+{
+    const int64_t DOF_WAIST = 3;
+    const int64_t DOF_NECK = 3;
+    const int64_t DOF_ARM = 14;
+    const int64_t DOF_LEG = 12;
+    const int64_t DOF_ALL = 32;
+
+    int64_t counter;
+    double joint_torque[DOF_ALL];
+    double joint_stiffness[DOF_ALL];
+    double joint_position[DOF_ALL];
+    double joint_damping[DOF_ALL];
+    double joint_velocity[DOF_ALL];
+}

+   <library code="--[[ Helper function to create a series from arrays&#xa;&#xa; new_series: a series previously created with ScatterXY.new(name)&#xa; prefix:     prefix of the timeseries, before the index of the array&#xa; suffix_X:   suffix to complete the name of the series containing the X value. If [nil], use the index of the array.&#xa; suffix_Y:   suffix to complete the name of the series containing the Y value&#xa; timestamp:   usually the tracker_time variable&#xa;              &#xa; Example:&#xa; &#xa; Assuming we have multiple series in the form:&#xa; &#xa;   /trajectory/node.{X}/position/x&#xa;   /trajectory/node.{X}/position/y&#xa;   &#xa; where {N} is the index of the array (integer). We can create a reactive series from the array with:&#xa; &#xa;   new_series = ScatterXY.new(&quot;my_trajectory&quot;) &#xa;   CreateSeriesFromArray( new_series, &quot;/trajectory/node&quot;, &quot;position/x&quot;, &quot;position/y&quot;, tracker_time );&#xa;--]]&#xa;&#xa;function CreateSeriesFromArray( new_series, prefix, suffix_X, suffix_Y, timestamp )&#xa;  &#xa;  --- clear previous values&#xa;  new_series:clear()&#xa;  &#xa;  --- Append points to new_series&#xa;  index = 0&#xa;  while(true) do&#xa;&#xa;    x = index;&#xa;    -- if not nil, get the X coordinate from a series&#xa;    if suffix_X ~= nil then &#xa;      series_x = TimeseriesView.find( string.format( &quot;%s.%d/%s&quot;, prefix, index, suffix_X) )&#xa;      if series_x == nil then break end&#xa;      x = series_x:atTime(timestamp)&#x9; &#xa;    end&#xa;    &#xa;    series_y = TimeseriesView.find( string.format( &quot;%s.%d/%s&quot;, prefix, index, suffix_Y) )&#xa;    if series_y == nil then break end &#xa;    y = series_y:atTime(timestamp)&#xa;    &#xa;    new_series:push_back(x,y)&#xa;    index = index+1&#xa;  end&#xa;end&#xa;&#xa;--[[ Similar to the built-in function GetSeriesNames(), but select only the names with a give prefix. --]]&#xa;&#xa;function GetSeriesNamesByPrefix(prefix)&#xa;  -- GetSeriesNames(9 is a built-in function&#xa;  all_names = GetSeriesNames()&#xa;  filtered_names = {}&#xa;  for i, name in ipairs(all_names)  do&#xa;    -- check the prefix&#xa;    if name:find(prefix, 1, #prefix) then&#xa;      table.insert(filtered_names, name);&#xa;    end&#xa;  end&#xa;  return filtered_names&#xa;end&#xa;&#xa;--[[ Modify an existing series, applying offsets to all their X and Y values&#xa;&#xa; series: an existing timeseries, obtained with TimeseriesView.find(name)&#xa; delta_x: offset to apply to each x value&#xa; delta_y: offset to apply to each y value &#xa;  &#xa;--]]&#xa;&#xa;function ApplyOffsetInPlace(series, delta_x, delta_y)&#xa;  -- use C++ indeces, not Lua indeces&#xa;  for index=0, series:size()-1 do&#xa;    x,y = series:at(index)&#xa;    series:set(index, x + delta_x, y + delta_y)&#xa;  end&#xa;end&#xa;"/>
