+from isaacgym import gymapi, gymutil, gymtorch
+from lcm import LCM
+from humanoid.test.cfg_r01_v111 import ConfigModule  # sim using issac gym
+from humanoid.test.msg.gen.lcm_r01_v111 import sim_t, usr_t, ctl_t
+
+# from prototype_controller.util import window_jumper
+# from prototype_controller.util.messenger_ros import MessengerRos
+import numpy as np
+import signal
+import sys
+import torch
+import warnings
+
+
+np.set_printoptions(linewidth=1000, precision=3, suppress=True)
+torch.set_printoptions(linewidth=1000, precision=3, sci_mode=False)
+warnings.simplefilter('always', UserWarning)
+
+
+class SimulatorModule:
+    def __init__(self):
+        # gym
+        self.gym = gymapi.acquire_gym()
+
+        # configuration
+        self.cfg = ConfigModule()
+
+        # lcm
+        self.lcm = LCM()
+        self.lcm.subscribe(self.cfg.ctl_lcm_topic_name, self.controller_handler)
+        self.msg_sim = sim_t()
+        self.msg_usr = usr_t()
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t()
+
+        # ros
+        # self.mr = MessengerRos(self.cfg.sim_ros_node_name)
+
+        # counter
+        self.counter = 0
+
+        # create sim
+        self.sim = self.gym.create_sim(0, 0, self.cfg.physics, self.cfg.sim_params)
+        self.sim_enabled = True
+
+        # create ground
+        self.gym.add_ground(self.sim, self.cfg.plane_params)
+
+        # create viewer
+        self.viewer = self.gym.create_viewer(self.sim, self.cfg.camera_properties)
+        self.events = []
+        for key, value in self.cfg.keyboard_event_dict.items():
+            self.gym.subscribe_viewer_keyboard_event(self.viewer, key, value)
+        self.event_shift = 1
+
+        # load asset
+        self.asset = self.gym.load_asset(self.sim, self.cfg.asset_root, self.cfg.asset_file, self.cfg.asset_options)
+        self.terrain = self.gym.load_asset(
+            self.sim, self.cfg.asset_root, self.cfg.terrain_file, self.cfg.terrain_options
+        )
+
+        self.dof_dict = self.gym.get_asset_dof_dict(self.asset)
+        self.rigid_body_dict = self.gym.get_asset_rigid_body_dict(self.asset)
+        self.joint_dict = self.gym.get_asset_joint_dict(self.asset)
+
+        self.pelvis_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.pelvis_name]
+        self.torso_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.torso_name]
+        self.head_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.head_name]
+        self.hand_index = [self.rigid_body_dict[name] for name in self.cfg.hand_name]
+        self.foot_index = [self.rigid_body_dict[name] for name in self.cfg.foot_name]
+
+        # position the camera
+        self.camera_tracking_enabled = self.cfg.camera_tracking_enabled
+        self.camera_pos = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos)
+        self.camera_pos_tgt = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.camera_abs_pose = gymapi.Transform()
+
+        # create env
+        env_lower = gymapi.Vec3()
+        env_upper = gymapi.Vec3()
+        num_per_row = 0
+        self.env = self.gym.create_env(self.sim, env_lower, env_upper, num_per_row)
+
+        pose = gymapi.Transform()
+        self.actor_handle = self.gym.create_actor(self.env, self.asset, pose, self.cfg.asset_name, 0, 1, 0)
+
+        self.dof_props = self.gym.get_actor_dof_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.dof_props["stiffness"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_stiffness)
+        self.dof_props["damping"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_damping)
+        self.dof_props["armature"] = self.cfg.dof_props_armature
+        self.dof_props["friction"] = self.cfg.dof_props_friction
+        self.dof_props["driveMode"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_drive_mode)
+        self.gym.set_actor_dof_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle, self.dof_props)
+        print(self.dof_props)
+
+        self.terrain_handle = self.gym.create_actor(self.env, self.terrain, pose, self.cfg.terrain_name, 0, 0, 0)
+        for i in range(self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_count(self.env, self.terrain_handle)):
+            self.gym.set_rigid_body_color(self.env, self.terrain_handle, i, gymapi.MESH_VISUAL, self.cfg.terrain_color)
+
+        self.rigid_body_props = self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.rigid_body_names = self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_names(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+
+        for i in range(len(self.rigid_body_props)):
+            self.rigid_body_props[i].mass *= 1
+            print(
+                self.rigid_body_names[i],
+                "\tmass = ",
+                self.rigid_body_props[i].mass,
+                "\tcom = ",
+                self.rigid_body_props[i].com,
+            )
+
+        self.total_mass = np.sum([self.rigid_body_props[i].mass for i in range(len(self.rigid_body_props))])
+        print("total mass = ", self.total_mass)
+        self.gym.set_actor_rigid_body_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle, self.rigid_body_props)
+
+        # prepare sim
+        self.gym.prepare_sim(self.sim)
+
+        # init tensor
+        self.pelvis_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.dof_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_dof_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.rigid_body_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_rigid_body_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.jacobian_tensor = self.gym.acquire_jacobian_tensor(self.sim, self.cfg.asset_name)
+        self.net_contact_force_tensor = self.gym.acquire_net_contact_force_tensor(self.sim)
+
+        self.pelvis_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.pelvis_state_tensor)
+        self.dof_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.dof_state_tensor)
+        self.rigid_body_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.rigid_body_state_tensor)
+        self.jacobian = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.jacobian_tensor)
+        self.net_contact_force = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.net_contact_force_tensor)
+
+        # init attractor
+        self.attractor_enabled = self.cfg.attractor_enabled
+        self.attractor_properties = gymapi.AttractorProperties()
+        self.attractor_properties.rigid_handle = self.gym.get_actor_root_rigid_body_handle(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+            gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+        )
+        self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.axes = gymapi.AXIS_ALL
+        self.attractor_handle = self.gym.create_rigid_body_attractor(self.env, self.attractor_properties)
+
+        # init actor state
+        self.reset_actor()
+
+        # init controller
+        self.reset_ctl = True
+        self.reset_ctl_last = True
+
+        # move viewer window
+        # window_jumper.main()
+
+    def run(self):
+        while self.sim_enabled:
+            self.update_physics()
+            self.update_camera()
+            self.update_visual()
+            self.update_tensor()
+            # self.update_termination()
+            self.update_simulator_command()
+            self.update_simulator_state()
+            self.update_user_state()
+            self.update_message()
+            self.update_controller()
+            self.update_info()
+            self.update_counter()
+            # self.sync_frame_time()
+
+        print("Done")
+
+        self.gym.destroy_viewer(self.viewer)
+        self.gym.destroy_sim(self.sim)
+
+    def reset_all(self):
+        # self.reset_camera()
+        self.reset_attractor()
+        self.reset_msg()
+        self.reset_actor()
+        self.reset_controller()
+        self.counter = 0
+
+    def reset_camera(self):
+        # self.camera_tracking_enabled = self.cfg.camera_tracking_enabled
+        self.camera_pos = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos)
+        self.camera_pos_tgt = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+
+    def reset_attractor(self):
+        # self.attractor_properties = gymapi.AttractorProperties()
+        self.attractor_properties.rigid_handle = self.gym.get_actor_root_rigid_body_handle(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+            gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+        )
+        self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.axes = gymapi.AXIS_ALL
+        self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+
+    def reset_msg(self):
+        self.msg_sim = sim_t()
+        self.msg_usr = usr_t()
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t()
+
+    def reset_actor(self):
+        self.pelvis_state[0] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_pelvis_state).to(torch.float)
+        self.pelvis_state[1] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_terrain_state).to(torch.float)
+        self.dof_state[:, 0] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_joint_position).to(torch.float)
+        self.dof_state[:, 1] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_joint_velocity).to(torch.float)
+
+        self.gym.set_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(self.pelvis_state))
+        self.gym.set_dof_state_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(self.dof_state))
+        self.update_tensor()
+
+    def reset_controller(self):
+        self.reset_ctl = True
+
+    def update_physics(self):
+        self.gym.simulate(self.sim)
+        self.gym.fetch_results(self.sim, True)
+
+    def update_camera(self):
+        if self.camera_tracking_enabled:
+            self.camera_pos_tgt.x = self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+            self.camera_pos_tgt.y = self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+            self.camera_pos.x = self.camera_abs_pose.p.x + self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+            self.camera_pos.y = self.camera_abs_pose.p.y + self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+            # self.camera_pos.z = self.camera_abs_pose.p.z + self.pelvis_state[0, 2]
+            self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+
+            if self.cfg.camera_tracking_once:
+                self.camera_tracking_enabled ^= True
+
+    def update_visual(self):
+        self.sim_enabled = not self.gym.query_viewer_has_closed(self.viewer)
+
+        self.gym.clear_lines(self.viewer)
+        self.draw_lines()
+
+        self.gym.step_graphics(self.sim)
+        self.gym.draw_viewer(self.viewer, self.sim, True)
+
+        self.events = self.gym.query_viewer_action_events(self.viewer)
+
+    def update_tensor(self):
+        self.gym.refresh_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_dof_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_rigid_body_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_jacobian_tensors(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_net_contact_force_tensor(self.sim)
+
+    def update_termination(self):
+        if (
+            self.pelvis_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.dof_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.rigid_body_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.jacobian.isnan().any()
+            or self.net_contact_force.isnan().any()
+        ):
+            self.reset_actor()
+            print(
+                "terminated, nan check "
+                + "[root_state, dof_state, rigid_body_state, jacobian, net_contact_force] = {}".format(
+                    [
+                        self.pelvis_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.dof_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.rigid_body_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.jacobian.isnan().any(),
+                        self.net_contact_force.isnan().any(),
+                    ]
+                )
+            )
+
+        max_distance = np.inf
+        max_height = 10
+        max_pitch_roll = np.deg2rad(60)
+        max_joint_vel = 30
+
+        xy_distance_check = np.linalg.norm(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[0:2]) > max_distance
+        z_height_check = np.abs(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[2]) > max_height
+        orientation_check = np.any(np.abs(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[3:5]) * 2 > max_pitch_roll)
+        joint_vel_check = np.any(np.abs([self.msg_sim.dof_state[i][1] for i in range(10)]) > max_joint_vel)
+
+        if np.any([xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check]):
+            self.reset_all()
+            print(
+                "terminated, [xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check] = {}".format(
+                    [xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check]
+                )
+            )
+
+    def update_simulator_command(self):
+        for evt in self.events:
+            if evt.action == "RESET_ALL" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.reset_all()
+            if evt.action == "RESET_ACTOR" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.reset_actor()
+                self.reset_controller()
+            elif evt.action == "ESCAPE" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.sim_enabled = False
+            elif evt.action == "HOLD" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.attractor_enabled ^= True
+                self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+                self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "CAMERA" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.camera_tracking_enabled ^= True
+                self.camera_abs_pose = self.gym.get_viewer_camera_transform(self.viewer, self.env)
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.x -= self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.y -= self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.z -= self.pelvis_state[0, 2]
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, self.cfg.perturb_force_x)
+                print("apply front push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, -self.cfg.perturb_force_x)
+                print("apply back push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, self.cfg.perturb_force_y)
+                print("apply side push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB4" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, -self.cfg.perturb_force_y)
+                print("apply side push")
+
+            if evt.action == "STOP" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+                    gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+                )
+            elif evt.action == "UP" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.y += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "DOWN" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.y -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.z += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.z -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.x += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.x -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "STAND" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.p.z += 0.02
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "SIT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.p.z -= 0.02
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+
+    def update_simulator_state(self):
+        self.msg_sim.counter = self.counter
+
+        self.msg_sim.dof_state[:] = self.dof_state.numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.pelvis_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.torso_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.torso_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.head_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.head_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.hand_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.hand_jacobian_wld[:] = self.jacobian[0, self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_jacobian_wld[:] = self.jacobian[0, self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.hand_contact_force_wld[:] = self.net_contact_force[self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_contact_force_wld[:] = self.net_contact_force[self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+    def update_user_state(self):
+        if self.reset_ctl_last:
+            self.reset_ctl = False
+        self.msg_usr.reset = self.reset_ctl_last = self.reset_ctl
+
+        for evt in self.events:
+            if evt.action == "ZERO_TORQUE" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.no_torque ^= True
+
+            if evt.action == "LEFT_SHIFT":
+                if evt.value > 0:
+                    self.event_shift = -1
+                else:
+                    self.event_shift = 1
+
+            if evt.action == "STOP" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value = [0 if i in {0, 1, 3, 4, 5} else self.msg_usr.joy_value[i] for i in range(7)]
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "UP" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] = np.minimum(2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "DOWN" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] = np.maximum(-1.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] = np.minimum(2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] = np.maximum(-2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] = np.minimum(0.5, self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] = np.maximum(-0.5, self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "STAND" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] = np.minimum(0.2, self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] + 0.02)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "SIT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] = np.maximum(-0.4, self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] - 0.02)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+
+            if evt.action == "0" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 0
+            elif evt.action == "1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 1
+            elif evt.action == "2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 2
+            elif evt.action == "3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 3
+            elif evt.action == "SMART_GAIT" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 4
+
+            if evt.action == "NUMPAD_0" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt = [[0.0 for dim1 in range(6)] for dim0 in range(2)]
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt = [0.0 for dim0 in range(2)]
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt = [[0.0 for dim1 in range(7)] for dim0 in range(2)]
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][0] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][0] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][1] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][1] -= self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][1] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][1] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][2] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][2] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][2] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][2] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_4" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][3] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][3] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][3] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][3] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_5" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][4] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][4] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][4] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][4] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_6" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][5] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_7" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt[0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt[1] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][6] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][6] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_8" and evt.value > 0:
+                pass
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_9" and evt.value > 0:
+                pass
+
+    def update_message(self):
+        self.lcm.publish(self.cfg.sim_lcm_topic_name, self.msg_sim.encode())
+        self.lcm.publish(self.cfg.usr_lcm_topic_name, self.msg_usr.encode())
+
+        try:
+            self.lcm.handle()
+            while self.lcm.handle_timeout(0):
+                warnings.warn("get repeated ctl message at counter {}".format(self.counter))
+        except OSError:
+            warnings.warn("No lcm", UserWarning)
+
+    def update_controller(self):
+        # Get the controller commands
+        joint_torque_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_torque) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_stiffness_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_stiffness) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_pos_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_position) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_damping_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_damping) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_vel_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_velocity) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+
+        # Calculate the combined joint torque command (Hybrid)
+        joint_pos = self.dof_state[:, 0].numpy()
+        joint_vel = self.dof_state[:, 1].numpy()
+        combined_joint_torque_cmd = (
+            joint_torque_cmd
+            - joint_stiffness_cmd * (joint_pos - joint_pos_cmd)
+            - joint_damping_cmd * (joint_vel - joint_vel_cmd)
+        )
+        # Calculate the combined joint torque command (Compensate the joint damping)
+        # this will make the system stable and in pure torque mode
+        # joint_vel = self.dof_state[:, 1].numpy()
+        # combined_joint_torque_cmd = joint_torque_cmd + self.dof_props["damping"] * joint_vel
+
+        # convert to gym tensor and send to gym
+        torch_combined_joint_torque = torch.from_numpy(combined_joint_torque_cmd).to(torch.float)
+        self.gym.set_dof_actuation_force_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(torch_combined_joint_torque))
+
+    def update_info(self):
+        pass
+
+    def update_counter(self):
+        self.counter += 1
+
+    def sync_frame_time(self):
+        # Wait for dt to elapse in real time.
+        # This synchronizes the physics simulation with the rendering rate.
+        self.gym.sync_frame_time(self.sim)
+
+    def draw_lines(self):
+        # draw foot connection
+        p1_index = self.foot_index[0]
+        p2_index = self.foot_index[1]
+
+        p1 = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, p1_index)
+        p2 = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, p2_index)
+        color = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.color_green)
+        gymutil.draw_line(p1.p, p2.p, color, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env)
+
+        # draw root that projects on the ground
+        pelvis_project_pose = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, 0)
+        # pelvis_project_pose.p.z = self.cfg.foot_radius + self.terrain_height
+        pelvis_project_pose.p.z = 0
+        gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_red, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pelvis_project_pose)
+
+        # Draw GRF
+        foot_contact_force = self.net_contact_force[self.foot_index].numpy()
+        for i in range(2):
+            pi = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, self.foot_index[i])
+            color = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.color_red)
+            gymutil.draw_line(
+                pi.p, pi.p + gymapi.Vec3(*(0.002 * foot_contact_force[i])), color, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env
+            )
+
+            # If in contact, draw red if not in contact draw blue
+            if np.linalg.norm(foot_contact_force[i]) > 0:
+                gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_red, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pi)
+            else:
+                gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_blue, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pi)
+
+    def controller_handler(self, channel, data):
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t.decode(data)
+
+
+def sigint_handler(signal_num, stack_frame):
+    # pycharm debugger stop with SIGINIT instead of SIGKILL
+    # kill all processes gracefully
+    print("killed by " + signal.Signals(signal_num).name)
+    sys.exit(0)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, sigint_handler)
+
+    app = SimulatorModule()
+    app.run()

+from isaacgym import gymapi, gymutil, gymtorch
+from lcm import LCM
+from humanoid.test.cfg_r01_v12 import ConfigModule  # sim using issac gym
+from humanoid.test.msg.gen.lcm_r01_v12 import sim_t, usr_t, ctl_t
+
+# from prototype_controller.util import window_jumper
+# from prototype_controller.util.messenger_ros import MessengerRos
+import numpy as np
+import signal
+import sys
+import torch
+import warnings
+
+
+np.set_printoptions(linewidth=1000, precision=3, suppress=True)
+torch.set_printoptions(linewidth=1000, precision=3, sci_mode=False)
+warnings.simplefilter('always', UserWarning)

+class SimulatorModule:
+    def __init__(self):
+        # gym
+        self.gym = gymapi.acquire_gym()
+
+        # configuration
+        self.cfg = ConfigModule()
+
+        # lcm
+        self.lcm = LCM()
+        self.lcm.subscribe(self.cfg.ctl_lcm_topic_name, self.controller_handler)
+        self.msg_sim = sim_t()
+        self.msg_usr = usr_t()
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t()
+
+        # ros
+        # self.mr = MessengerRos(self.cfg.sim_ros_node_name)
+
+        # counter
+        self.counter = 0
+
+        # create sim
+        self.sim = self.gym.create_sim(0, 0, self.cfg.physics, self.cfg.sim_params)
+        self.sim_enabled = True
+
+        # create ground
+        self.gym.add_ground(self.sim, self.cfg.plane_params)
+
+        # create viewer
+        self.viewer = self.gym.create_viewer(self.sim, self.cfg.camera_properties)
+        self.events = []
+        for key, value in self.cfg.keyboard_event_dict.items():
+            self.gym.subscribe_viewer_keyboard_event(self.viewer, key, value)
+        self.event_shift = 1
+
+        # load asset
+        self.asset = self.gym.load_asset(self.sim, self.cfg.asset_root, self.cfg.asset_file, self.cfg.asset_options)
+        self.terrain = self.gym.load_asset(
+            self.sim, self.cfg.asset_root, self.cfg.terrain_file, self.cfg.terrain_options
+        )
+
+        self.dof_dict = self.gym.get_asset_dof_dict(self.asset)
+        self.rigid_body_dict = self.gym.get_asset_rigid_body_dict(self.asset)
+        self.joint_dict = self.gym.get_asset_joint_dict(self.asset)
+
+        self.pelvis_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.pelvis_name]
+        self.torso_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.torso_name]
+        self.head_index = self.rigid_body_dict[self.cfg.head_name]
+        self.hand_index = [self.rigid_body_dict[name] for name in self.cfg.hand_name]
+        self.foot_index = [self.rigid_body_dict[name] for name in self.cfg.foot_name]
+
+        # position the camera
+        self.camera_tracking_enabled = self.cfg.camera_tracking_enabled
+        self.camera_pos = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos)
+        self.camera_pos_tgt = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.camera_abs_pose = gymapi.Transform()
+
+        # create env
+        env_lower = gymapi.Vec3()
+        env_upper = gymapi.Vec3()
+        num_per_row = 0
+        self.env = self.gym.create_env(self.sim, env_lower, env_upper, num_per_row)
+
+        pose = gymapi.Transform()
+        self.actor_handle = self.gym.create_actor(self.env, self.asset, pose, self.cfg.asset_name, 0, 1, 0)
+
+        self.dof_props = self.gym.get_actor_dof_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.dof_props["stiffness"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_stiffness)
+        self.dof_props["damping"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_damping)
+        self.dof_props["armature"] = self.cfg.dof_props_armature
+        self.dof_props["friction"] = self.cfg.dof_props_friction
+        self.dof_props["driveMode"].fill(self.cfg.dof_props_drive_mode)
+        self.gym.set_actor_dof_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle, self.dof_props)
+        print(self.dof_props)
+
+        self.terrain_handle = self.gym.create_actor(self.env, self.terrain, pose, self.cfg.terrain_name, 0, 0, 0)
+        for i in range(self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_count(self.env, self.terrain_handle)):
+            self.gym.set_rigid_body_color(self.env, self.terrain_handle, i, gymapi.MESH_VISUAL, self.cfg.terrain_color)
+
+        self.rigid_body_props = self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.rigid_body_names = self.gym.get_actor_rigid_body_names(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+
+        for i in range(len(self.rigid_body_props)):
+            self.rigid_body_props[i].mass *= 1
+            print(
+                self.rigid_body_names[i],
+                "\tmass = ",
+                self.rigid_body_props[i].mass,
+                "\tcom = ",
+                self.rigid_body_props[i].com,
+            )
+
+        self.total_mass = np.sum([self.rigid_body_props[i].mass for i in range(len(self.rigid_body_props))])
+        print("total mass = ", self.total_mass)
+        self.gym.set_actor_rigid_body_properties(self.env, self.actor_handle, self.rigid_body_props)
+
+        # prepare sim
+        self.gym.prepare_sim(self.sim)
+
+        # init tensor
+        self.pelvis_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.dof_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_dof_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.rigid_body_state_tensor = self.gym.acquire_rigid_body_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.jacobian_tensor = self.gym.acquire_jacobian_tensor(self.sim, self.cfg.asset_name)
+        self.net_contact_force_tensor = self.gym.acquire_net_contact_force_tensor(self.sim)
+
+        self.pelvis_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.pelvis_state_tensor)
+        self.dof_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.dof_state_tensor)
+        self.rigid_body_state = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.rigid_body_state_tensor)
+        self.jacobian = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.jacobian_tensor)
+        self.net_contact_force = gymtorch.wrap_tensor(self.net_contact_force_tensor)
+
+        # init attractor
+        self.attractor_enabled = self.cfg.attractor_enabled
+        self.attractor_properties = gymapi.AttractorProperties()
+        self.attractor_properties.rigid_handle = self.gym.get_actor_root_rigid_body_handle(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+            gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+        )
+        self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.axes = gymapi.AXIS_ALL
+        self.attractor_handle = self.gym.create_rigid_body_attractor(self.env, self.attractor_properties)
+
+        # init actor state
+        self.reset_actor()
+
+        # init controller
+        self.reset_ctl = True
+        self.reset_ctl_last = True
+
+        # move viewer window
+        # window_jumper.main()
+
+    def run(self):
+        while self.sim_enabled:
+            self.update_physics()
+            self.update_camera()
+            self.update_visual()
+            self.update_tensor()
+            # self.update_termination()
+            self.update_simulator_command()
+            self.update_simulator_state()
+            self.update_user_state()
+            self.update_message()
+            self.update_controller()
+            self.update_info()
+            self.update_counter()
+            # self.sync_frame_time()
+
+        print("Done")
+
+        self.gym.destroy_viewer(self.viewer)
+        self.gym.destroy_sim(self.sim)
+
+    def reset_all(self):
+        # self.reset_camera()
+        self.reset_attractor()
+        self.reset_msg()
+        self.reset_actor()
+        self.reset_controller()
+        self.counter = 0
+
+    def reset_camera(self):
+        # self.camera_tracking_enabled = self.cfg.camera_tracking_enabled
+        self.camera_pos = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos)
+        self.camera_pos_tgt = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.camera_pos_tgt)
+        self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+
+    def reset_attractor(self):
+        # self.attractor_properties = gymapi.AttractorProperties()
+        self.attractor_properties.rigid_handle = self.gym.get_actor_root_rigid_body_handle(self.env, self.actor_handle)
+        self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+            gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+        )
+        self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+        self.attractor_properties.axes = gymapi.AXIS_ALL
+        self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+
+    def reset_msg(self):
+        self.msg_sim = sim_t()
+        self.msg_usr = usr_t()
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t()
+
+    def reset_actor(self):
+        self.pelvis_state[0] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_pelvis_state).to(torch.float)
+        self.pelvis_state[1] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_terrain_state).to(torch.float)
+        self.dof_state[:, 0] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_joint_position).to(torch.float)
+        self.dof_state[:, 1] = torch.from_numpy(self.cfg.init_joint_velocity).to(torch.float)
+
+        self.gym.set_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(self.pelvis_state))
+        self.gym.set_dof_state_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(self.dof_state))
+        self.update_tensor()
+
+    def reset_controller(self):
+        self.reset_ctl = True
+
+    def update_physics(self):
+        self.gym.simulate(self.sim)
+        self.gym.fetch_results(self.sim, True)
+
+    def update_camera(self):
+        if self.camera_tracking_enabled:
+            self.camera_pos_tgt.x = self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+            self.camera_pos_tgt.y = self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+            self.camera_pos.x = self.camera_abs_pose.p.x + self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+            self.camera_pos.y = self.camera_abs_pose.p.y + self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+            # self.camera_pos.z = self.camera_abs_pose.p.z + self.pelvis_state[0, 2]
+            self.gym.viewer_camera_look_at(self.viewer, None, self.camera_pos, self.camera_pos_tgt)
+
+            if self.cfg.camera_tracking_once:
+                self.camera_tracking_enabled ^= True
+
+    def update_visual(self):
+        self.sim_enabled = not self.gym.query_viewer_has_closed(self.viewer)
+
+        self.gym.clear_lines(self.viewer)
+        self.draw_lines()
+
+        self.gym.step_graphics(self.sim)
+        self.gym.draw_viewer(self.viewer, self.sim, True)
+
+        self.events = self.gym.query_viewer_action_events(self.viewer)
+
+    def update_tensor(self):
+        self.gym.refresh_actor_root_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_dof_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_rigid_body_state_tensor(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_jacobian_tensors(self.sim)
+        self.gym.refresh_net_contact_force_tensor(self.sim)
+
+    def update_termination(self):
+        if (
+            self.pelvis_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.dof_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.rigid_body_state.isnan().any()
+            or self.jacobian.isnan().any()
+            or self.net_contact_force.isnan().any()
+        ):
+            self.reset_actor()
+            print(
+                "terminated, nan check "
+                + "[root_state, dof_state, rigid_body_state, jacobian, net_contact_force] = {}".format(
+                    [
+                        self.pelvis_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.dof_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.rigid_body_state.isnan().any(),
+                        self.jacobian.isnan().any(),
+                        self.net_contact_force.isnan().any(),
+                    ]
+                )
+            )
+
+        max_distance = np.inf
+        max_height = 10
+        max_pitch_roll = np.deg2rad(60)
+        max_joint_vel = 30
+
+        xy_distance_check = np.linalg.norm(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[0:2]) > max_distance
+        z_height_check = np.abs(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[2]) > max_height
+        orientation_check = np.any(np.abs(self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[3:5]) * 2 > max_pitch_roll)
+        joint_vel_check = np.any(np.abs([self.msg_sim.dof_state[i][1] for i in range(10)]) > max_joint_vel)
+
+        if np.any([xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check]):
+            self.reset_all()
+            print(
+                "terminated, [xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check] = {}".format(
+                    [xy_distance_check, z_height_check, orientation_check, joint_vel_check]
+                )
+            )
+
+    def update_simulator_command(self):
+        for evt in self.events:
+            if evt.action == "RESET_ALL" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.reset_all()
+            if evt.action == "RESET_ACTOR" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.reset_actor()
+                self.reset_controller()
+            elif evt.action == "ESCAPE" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.sim_enabled = False
+            elif evt.action == "HOLD" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.attractor_enabled ^= True
+                self.attractor_properties.stiffness = 1e6 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+                self.attractor_properties.damping = 1e4 if self.attractor_enabled else 0
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "CAMERA" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.camera_tracking_enabled ^= True
+                self.camera_abs_pose = self.gym.get_viewer_camera_transform(self.viewer, self.env)
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.x -= self.pelvis_state[0, 0]
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.y -= self.pelvis_state[0, 1]
+                self.camera_abs_pose.p.z -= self.pelvis_state[0, 2]
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, self.cfg.perturb_force_x)
+                print("apply front push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, -self.cfg.perturb_force_x)
+                print("apply back push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, self.cfg.perturb_force_y)
+                print("apply side push")
+            elif evt.action == "PERTURB4" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.gym.apply_body_force_at_pos(self.env, self.pelvis_index, -self.cfg.perturb_force_y)
+                print("apply side push")
+
+            if evt.action == "STOP" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target = gymapi.Transform(
+                    gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[0:3]), gymapi.Quat(*self.cfg.init_pelvis_state[3:7])
+                )
+            elif evt.action == "UP" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.y += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "DOWN" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.y -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.z += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.z -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.x += np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.r.x -= np.deg2rad(10) / 2  # quat = euler / 2
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "STAND" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.p.z += 0.02
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+            elif evt.action == "SIT" and evt.value > 0 and self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.attractor_properties.target.p.z -= 0.02
+                self.gym.set_attractor_properties(self.env, self.attractor_handle, self.attractor_properties)
+
+    def update_simulator_state(self):
+        self.msg_sim.counter = self.counter
+
+        self.msg_sim.dof_state[:] = self.dof_state.numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.pelvis_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.pelvis_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.torso_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.torso_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.head_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.head_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.hand_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_state[:] = self.rigid_body_state[self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.torso_jacobian_wld[:] = self.jacobian[0, self.torso_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.hand_jacobian_wld[:] = self.jacobian[0, self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_jacobian_wld[:] = self.jacobian[0, self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+        self.msg_sim.hand_contact_force_wld[:] = self.net_contact_force[self.hand_index].numpy().tolist()
+        self.msg_sim.foot_contact_force_wld[:] = self.net_contact_force[self.foot_index].numpy().tolist()
+
+    def update_user_state(self):
+        if self.reset_ctl_last:
+            self.reset_ctl = False
+        self.msg_usr.reset = self.reset_ctl_last = self.reset_ctl
+
+        for evt in self.events:
+            if evt.action == "ZERO_TORQUE" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.no_torque ^= True
+
+            if evt.action == "LEFT_SHIFT":
+                if evt.value > 0:
+                    self.event_shift = -1
+                else:
+                    self.event_shift = 1
+
+            if evt.action == "STOP" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value = [0 if i in {0, 1, 3, 4, 5} else self.msg_usr.joy_value[i] for i in range(7)]
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "UP" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] = np.minimum(2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "DOWN" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] = np.maximum(-1.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[0] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] = np.minimum(2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "TURN_RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] = np.maximum(-2.0, self.msg_usr.joy_value[5] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "LEFT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] = np.minimum(0.5, self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] + 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "RIGHT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] = np.maximum(-0.5, self.msg_usr.joy_value[1] - 0.1)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "STAND" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] = np.minimum(0.2, self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] + 0.02)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+            elif evt.action == "SIT" and evt.value > 0 and not self.attractor_enabled:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] = np.maximum(-0.4, self.msg_usr.joy_value[2] - 0.02)
+                print("joy_value = {}".format(self.msg_usr.joy_value))
+
+            if evt.action == "0" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 0
+            elif evt.action == "1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 1
+            elif evt.action == "2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 2
+            elif evt.action == "3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 3
+            elif evt.action == "SMART_GAIT" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.joy_value[6] = 4
+
+            if evt.action == "NUMPAD_0" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt = [[0.0 for dim1 in range(6)] for dim0 in range(2)]
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt = [0.0 for dim0 in range(2)]
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt = [[0.0 for dim1 in range(7)] for dim0 in range(2)]
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_1" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][0] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][0] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_2" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][1] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][1] -= self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][1] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][1] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_3" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][2] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][2] += self.event_shift * 0.1
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][2] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][2] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_4" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][3] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][3] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][3] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][3] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_5" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][4] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][4] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][4] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][4] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_6" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[0][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.hand_tgt[1][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][5] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][5] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_7" and evt.value > 0:
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt[0] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.j3_tgt[1] -= self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[0][6] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+                self.msg_usr.arm_pos_tgt[1][6] += self.event_shift * np.deg2rad(10)
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_8" and evt.value > 0:
+                pass
+            elif evt.action == "NUMPAD_9" and evt.value > 0:
+                pass
+
+    def update_message(self):
+        self.lcm.publish(self.cfg.sim_lcm_topic_name, self.msg_sim.encode())
+        self.lcm.publish(self.cfg.usr_lcm_topic_name, self.msg_usr.encode())
+
+        try:
+            self.lcm.handle()
+            while self.lcm.handle_timeout(0):
+                warnings.warn("get repeated ctl message at counter {}".format(self.counter))
+        except OSError:
+            warnings.warn("No lcm", UserWarning)
+
+    def update_controller(self):
+        # Get the controller commands
+        joint_torque_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_torque) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_stiffness_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_stiffness) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_pos_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_position) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_damping_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_damping) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+        joint_vel_cmd = (
+            np.array(self.msg_ctl.joint_velocity) if self.msg_ctl.counter > 0 else np.zeros(self.cfg.dof_joint)
+        )
+
+        # Calculate the combined joint torque command (Hybrid)
+        joint_pos = self.dof_state[:, 0].numpy()
+        joint_vel = self.dof_state[:, 1].numpy()
+        combined_joint_torque_cmd = (
+            joint_torque_cmd
+            - joint_stiffness_cmd * (joint_pos - joint_pos_cmd)
+            - joint_damping_cmd * (joint_vel - joint_vel_cmd)
+        )
+        # Calculate the combined joint torque command (Compensate the joint damping)
+        # this will make the system stable and in pure torque mode
+        # joint_vel = self.dof_state[:, 1].numpy()
+        # combined_joint_torque_cmd = joint_torque_cmd + self.dof_props["damping"] * joint_vel
+
+        # convert to gym tensor and send to gym
+        torch_combined_joint_torque = torch.from_numpy(combined_joint_torque_cmd).to(torch.float)
+        self.gym.set_dof_actuation_force_tensor(self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(torch_combined_joint_torque))
+
+    def update_info(self):
+        pass
+
+    def update_counter(self):
+        self.counter += 1
+
+    def sync_frame_time(self):
+        # Wait for dt to elapse in real time.
+        # This synchronizes the physics simulation with the rendering rate.
+        self.gym.sync_frame_time(self.sim)
+
+    def draw_lines(self):
+        # draw foot connection
+        p1_index = self.foot_index[0]
+        p2_index = self.foot_index[1]
+
+        p1 = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, p1_index)
+        p2 = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, p2_index)
+        color = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.color_green)
+        gymutil.draw_line(p1.p, p2.p, color, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env)
+
+        # draw root that projects on the ground
+        pelvis_project_pose = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, 0)
+        # pelvis_project_pose.p.z = self.cfg.foot_radius + self.terrain_height
+        pelvis_project_pose.p.z = 0
+        gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_red, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pelvis_project_pose)
+
+        # Draw GRF
+        foot_contact_force = self.net_contact_force[self.foot_index].numpy()
+        for i in range(2):
+            pi = self.gym.get_rigid_transform(self.env, self.foot_index[i])
+            color = gymapi.Vec3(*self.cfg.color_red)
+            gymutil.draw_line(
+                pi.p, pi.p + gymapi.Vec3(*(0.002 * foot_contact_force[i])), color, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env
+            )
+
+            # If in contact, draw red if not in contact draw blue
+            if np.linalg.norm(foot_contact_force[i]) > 0:
+                gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_red, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pi)
+            else:
+                gymutil.draw_lines(self.cfg.sphere_blue, self.gym, self.viewer, self.env, pi)
+
+    def controller_handler(self, channel, data):
+        self.msg_ctl = ctl_t.decode(data)
+
+
+def sigint_handler(signal_num, stack_frame):
+    # pycharm debugger stop with SIGINIT instead of SIGKILL
+    # kill all processes gracefully
+    print("killed by " + signal.Signals(signal_num).name)
+    sys.exit(0)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, sigint_handler)
+
+    app = SimulatorModule()
+    app.run()
